法國會通過造艦程序

▲Paris, 18th (National Press) - The French parliament has passed the 1932 naval construction program. This plan requires a total expenditure of 1,216,000,000,000 francs, to build eight new warships, including four 7,500-ton cruisers. Although France is complying with the naval construction moratorium proposed by the participating nations at the League of Nations, its moratorium only applies to the completion of new warships, and therefore does not conflict with the current naval construction program passed. The French parliament had previously passed a naval construction plan before the summer recess; this is the second time. Furthermore, the naval construction program based on the Five-Power Treaty of the Washington Naval Conference in 1924 is still ongoing. This program stipulates that 240,000 tons of new warships will be built by the end of 1936, with 196,799 tons replacing old warships. Although France is currently preparing for disarmament, Foreign Minister Briand solemnly declared to the League of Nations that France's reduction of armaments must be proportional to the guarantee of security it receives. In essence, this means that without a guarantee of military assistance, France cannot reduce its armaments. The French claim that France is the last country among the great powers capable of defending against the spread of communism in Europe, and therefore must have adequate naval and land forces to uphold its political主張.

美衆院附修正核准停債計畫

▲Washington, 18th (Reuters) - The House of Representatives today passed President Hoover's one-year war debt moratorium proposal by a vote of 317 to 100, with an amendment stating that canceling or reducing foreign debt is against the policy of Congress.

意閣將有重要更動

▲Berlin, 18th (National Press) - Before Christmas, there will be significant changes in the Italian cabinet. Several cabinet members will resign, but Foreign Minister Grandi is highly trusted by Prime Minister Mussolini and will not be transferred.

德著名冶金廠停頓

受經濟恐慌影響

▲Berlin, 18th (Reuters) - The renowned German Borsig Machine Factory has suspended payments today due to low orders and significant losses in overseas business caused by currency depreciation. However, the suspension is limited to the Borsig factory in Berlin and does not affect the parent company, which has factories and mines in Upper Silesia. This factory was established 80 years ago, and 80% of its products are sold to India, Egypt, and the Far East, employing 4,000 workers. It is hoped that work can be maintained until February of next year, as there are still orders worth millions of marks that have not yet been delivered. In addition, the famous Thyssen ironworks will also suspend work for two weeks from December 20th due to a lack of orders.

▲Berlin, 18th (Havas) - Another company has been added to the list of German industrial circles suffering from economic and financial panic today. The Borsig Metallurgical Factory, which manufactures locomotives in the suburbs of Berlin, has recently suspended payments. The factory has 3,700 workers and employees and is quite large. It is currently engaged in negotiations to try to save it. Apart from Krupp, this factory is one of the leading private metallurgical companies in Germany, founded in 1837 by the locksmith August Borsig. The first German locomotive was built by this factory in 1841.

唐古倫黨陰謀暴動

斐當道預有戒備

▲Manila, 19th (Reuters) - The Tanggulang Party, composed of disgruntled people from the provinces of the Philippines, had previously planned to gather in Manila on December 18th to join forces with the bandit party of Fu Di to attack various government administrative offices. However, as of today, the Tanggulang Party's plan to attack Manila has not materialized, reportedly due to the fact that the party members in the province of Rizal have not yet completed their preparations. Yesterday, the whole city was in panic, and all the Chinese shops closed early to prevent looting. Today, the police are still seriously patrolling the key areas leading into Manila, with troops stationed to prevent party members from breaking in. The customs authorities have also dispatched motor launches to patrol the Pasig River to prevent party members from invading by waterway. The leader of the party, Almajara, was previously detained and released on bail, and was arrested and imprisoned again yesterday. The authorities will charge him with treason.

蘇俄改進報紙宣傳

▲Moscow, 18th (National Press) - According to a recent announcement from the Central Committee of the Communist Party, the party's propaganda organ, Pravda, will start printing the same newspaper in fourteen major cities from January 1st of next year. This is one of the party's newly established propaganda plans and is closely related to the Five-Year Plan. According to the new plan, the newspaper's daily circulation will increase to over four million in the future. The printing method involves delivering various news items to various cities by airplane, and then typesetting and printing them within a few hours for simultaneous publication. However, Pravda is not the largest newspaper. There is also a peasant newspaper that plans to adopt this delivery method, and its circulation will increase to five million copies. In addition, a semi-official newspaper called Izvestia will also implement the new plan, and its circulation will increase to 2.5 million copies. Furthermore, the construction of major Russian paper mills will be completed soon, and the paper produced will be sufficient for the expansion of major newspapers.

▲Leningrad, 18th (National Press) - The old capital of Russia is now showing signs of prosperity, surpassing Moscow. According to today's newspaper, population statistics show that Leningrad now has a total of 2,536,000 residents, making it the seventh most populous city in the world. Among them, about one million are laborers serving in 400 factories, and its output accounts for one-sixth of the total industrial output of the Soviet Union.

Guangzhou, Shi Qingyang et al. telegram - Respectfully to the Central Party Headquarters, the National Government Military Commission, all levels of party headquarters nationwide, all army general commanders and commanders, all army division and brigade commanders, all provincial and municipal governments, all mass organizations, all schools, and all newspapers. The Japanese bandits have penetrated deeply, and the situation in the Northeast is urgent. The French masters are eyeing the border, and frequent alarms are being sounded in the Southwest. Recently, we have received repeated telegrams stating that the French imperialists are scheming to invade along the Yunnan-Guangxi border, and the disaster is profound and urgent, no less than that of Japan. Please allow us to present this to the Central Party Headquarters, the National Government, the southwestern authorities, and the elders and brothers throughout the country: (1) On the 13th and 14th of last month, two French aircraft entered our airspace and flew to Longzhou to reconnoiter the situation. (2) After the Shenyang Incident, the French newspapers in Hanoi advocated for Japan, saying that Japan safeguards Western culture and treaty interests and can serve as a model for Europe. (3) According to a telegram from the 3rd of last month, France has completed the construction of an airfield in Liangshan, and troops have been increased in all border areas. (4) According to a telegram from the 28th of last month, the Vietnamese government, in addition to recruiting new soldiers, is also summoning retired soldiers from more than ten years ago for training in Hanoi, with a five-month term, preparing to be deployed to various locations. (5) The roads within Vietnam have been extended to our border areas of Ping而 and Shuikou, and the width of the roads has been expanded. In addition, barracks capable of accommodating a division have been built in Liangshan. (6) Vietnam has banned the export of grain this year and is absorbing cash. (7) On the 20th of last month, 70 or 80 French soldiers crossed the border without reason, attacked farmers in Gaolü Village, and looted wantonly. A few days ago, they also entered Aidian. French soldiers also entered Yunnan Province to harass. (8) According to a telegram from the 8th of this month, France transported cannons, rifles, ammunition, and 20,000 sets of military uniforms to Liangshan and distributed them to retired soldiers. (9) According to a telegram from Guangxi on the 9th of this month, the French have recently transported most of the troops from Africa to Vietnam, along with countless military equipment and supplies. The above are all confirmed news. In addition, there is news of British troops increasing their presence in Pianma. If our government and people do not quickly plan for defense and eliminate the hidden dangers, I fear that the southwestern territories will soon become a continuation of the three northeastern provinces. We, feeling that the situation is dangerous and urgent, cannot bear to sit idly by. Therefore, on the morning of the 12th of this month, we convened southwestern comrades at the Guangdong Provincial Party Headquarters to discuss countermeasures. We decided on six principles: (1) The southwestern provinces will work together to resist foreign aggression. (2) The National Government is requested to convene a southwest border defense conference immediately and establish a southwest border defense committee. (3) The National Government is requested to pre-allocate funds and equipment and to construct southwest border fortresses and complete southwest transportation in sections. (4) Actively organize the militia in the southwestern provinces to serve as the government's rear support against foreign aggression. (5) Strictly prevent internal traitors from undermining the united action of the Southwest to resist foreign aggression. (6) Organize a foreign affairs association in the southwestern provinces, and immediately select people from each province to prepare everything, which can be announced soon. We deeply believe that the national crisis is deepening, dictatorship has not been overthrown, and the establishment of a unified government will take time. The officials in charge of our Southwest, having assumed the responsibility of defending the territory, should formulate a plan to protect the country. While there may be territorial divisions internally, there should be no distinction between each other in resisting foreign aggression. If they can quickly catch up, unite, adopt the principles decided by us today, adhere to strategies, rectify military preparations, train the people, gather talents, revitalize internal affairs, and promote transportation, then we will be prepared for any eventuality, consolidate border defenses, and will not be like Zhang Xueliang, who offered no resistance and willingly abandoned territory and lost power. We are extremely anxious in this telegram. Shi Qingyang, Yang Xingtao, Li Renren, Huang Jun, Huang Xiao, Xie Weiping, Yan Chongyang, Mo Jiying, Ma Yuechuan, Zhou Bogan, Huang Fusheng, Zhang Gan, Zhang Yunliang, Miao Ruoxu, Zhu Qingsheng, Xiao Shouyi, Huo Guanghe, Tang Dean, Huang Yixiang, Wei Renzhong, Yu Zuming, Wang Gongdu, Gao Xuan, Gong Zhilin, Yang Maozhang, Ming Wei Bei, Ou Fangpu, Su Minsheng, Li Qing, Du Zhiyuan, Su Shuyan, Zhang Mingjiu, Wang Suxi, Li Shishu, Chen Jingxiu, Wang Jundong, Yin Jianhua, Li Boshen, Yu Yunlan, Wu Zhaoxian, Guo Zihuo, Fang Naibin, Mo Yiyong, Wei Yong, Huang Yiduan, respectfully submit our document with seals.

日政府議建東省新行政區

▲採取統治朝鮮制度

▲軍部主設滿洲總督

▲推翻漢奸之維持會

Tokyo Correspondence: The Japanese government is currently studying the establishment of an administrative district in the Eastern Provinces and organizing the highest organ to govern Manchuria and Mongolia. Since Japan forcibly occupied the Eastern Provinces, it has repeatedly incited the Manchus to organize an independent government. However, due to the opposition of the general Chinese traitors, the restoration movement has become a bubble. The political power of Jilin and Liaoning is still executed by the "Four People's Maintenance Association" organized by Chinese traitors such as Yuan Jinkai. Recently, the government suddenly proposed to establish a new administrative district in the Eastern Provinces, overthrowing all the rights of the Chinese traitors, adopting the system of governing Korea and Taiwan, and not establishing an autonomous state by the Manchus. Regarding the implementation methods, the Japanese government has secretly studied with the military several times. According to the government's opinion, it wants to first organize a "Four Heads" government in the Eastern Provinces, with the Army, the Kwantung Government, the Consul General, and the South Manchuria Railway jointly forming the Manchuria-Mongolia Summit Conference, inviting the Governor-General of Korea to participate and prepare a plan for governing the Eastern Provinces. However, the military's Minister of the Army, Minami, has a slightly different opinion from the government, advocating expanding the powers of the Governor-General of Kwantung, with the government appointing a Governor-General stationed in Manchuria, or the government dispatching a high-ranking official similar to the Governor-General to be stationed in Manchuria, establishing an administrative district built by the Japanese themselves, and resolutely excluding the existing political power of the Chinese and Manchus in the Eastern Provinces. If this is because it is currently a time of military and political affairs with China, a Governor-General's Office can also be established in the Eastern Provinces, with a general-level figure as the head. The Governor-General's Office would be divided into two departments: a staff department and an administrative department. All Japanese troops stationed in Manchuria would be controlled by the Governor-General, and there would be no need to consult the government on matters. The administrative department would govern the provinces, cities, and counties of the Eastern Provinces and also manage all industries, transportation, and construction projects. Furthermore, in view of the disadvantages of the governance system between India and Korea, the military is resolutely advocating adopting a military system for the Eastern Provinces administrative district, opposing the "Four Heads" government proposed by Prime Minister Wakatsuki and Foreign Minister Shidehara. If either the Japanese government's or the military's proposal is established, the map of our country's Eastern Provinces will have practically changed, and the Japanese's long-standing ambition to occupy the Eastern Provinces will become even more evident. (December 14)

日機在錦擲彈

▲英美武官調查明確

▲日軍方面尚圖掩飾

Damei Evening News, Shenyang, December 18:

Page 12

Colonel Magee, military attaché of the U.S. Legation, and Colonel Sandys Hill, military attaché of the British Legation, have been residing in Jinzhou for the past three weeks, inspecting everything. They arrived here from Jinzhou this afternoon and stated that Japanese warplanes had dropped 26 bombs in the Jinzhou area, 23 of which caused much damage. This occurred within the past two days. However, the communique issued by Commander Honjo's headquarters did not mention this, only stating that Japanese reconnaissance planes had flown to Jinzhou to inspect the Zheng-Tong Railway's condition, as Japanese had invested in the railway. It was also stated that Japanese planes had dropped 18 bombs near Panshan, 17 of which exploded. Colonel Magee personally inspected the locations where the bombs had landed and saw that each bomb weighed about 200 pounds and was deeply embedded in the ice-covered ground. He estimated that the material damage was minimal and that no one was killed or injured. Both Colonel Magee and Colonel Sandys Hill emphatically denied the claim that Chinese soldiers near Jinzhou had increased in number, and they denied the claim made by the Japanese military headquarters here that Chinese troops were advancing towards Shenyang. They stated that the Chinese troops in Jinzhou had absolutely no intention of invading, and were only seeking a place to sleep at night and a full meal during the day. Even the stragglers entering the villages between Jinzhou and Shenyang were only trying to find food and lodging and had no intention of provoking the Japanese soldiers. The claim that Zhang Xueliang was funding so-called guerrillas to harass the Japanese along the South Manchuria Railway was also deemed incredible. The two officers, Magee and Sandys Hill, have scheduled a meeting with Commander Honjo tomorrow morning, but the purpose of the meeting is unknown. Today, the Japanese military authorities also announced that there were bandits near Shenyang and Changchun, one of whom was a group of bandits who kidnapped 70 Chinese women with the intention of extorting ransoms. This statement has not been verified. It was also stated that there are currently 8,000 Chinese troops gathered at Baiqibao, west of Xinmin.

外艦潛赴粤海岸測量

▲偷攝地形測量水線

▲當局派艦實力制止

Guangzhou Correspondence: While the external troubles are becoming more urgent and the northeast region has attracted the attention of the world, at the same time, the southwestern frontier is also coveted by foreigners. Taking advantage of our increasingly urgent external troubles, the ambition of foreigners has recently become unrestrained. The authorities have been reporting for days that foreign warships have been found secretly taking photographs of the terrain and measuring the harbors of Chixi and Yamen on the southern coast. According to Jiang Qihua, the magistrate of Chixi County, at 11:00 a.m. on the 2nd of this month, a large white ship with a yellow chimney, resembling a Japanese warship, was discovered in the waters off Huangmao Island in the county, sailing around and taking measurements. It left at 5:00 p.m. He immediately went to various parts of the coast to conduct on-site investigations and further learned that six of these warships had been sailing in the waters off Gaolan Island in the 8th district of Zhongshan County in the past two or three days and had planted many markers along the coast. The details are as follows: (1) On the mountain of Duya Island facing the sea of Baishi Township, Duhu District, Taishan County, there is a white cloth flag with a length of about one foot and a width of eight feet, with no characters. (2) On the highest peak of Gaolan Island in the 8th district of Zhongshan County, there is a black cloth flag of the same size as above, with no characters. (3) Also, at the foot of the mountain on the southern Jingkou coast of Gaolan Island, there is a wooden board with a width of eight inches and a height of more than eight feet, with no characters. (4) On Hesetu Mountain, which is distant from Gaolan Island, there is a black cloth flag of the same size as above. (5) On the high mountain of Dajin Island in the county, which is about fifty or sixty miles away from the county seat, there is a white cloth flag of the same size as above. Just as we were about to report, secret agents reported that a Japanese warship, white with a yellow chimney, was still hiding in the sea between Dajin Island in the county and Hebao Island in Zhongshan County, shining searchlights all night to spy on our coasts. After investigating, it is certain that the ship's secret entry into the interior seems to be taking measurements of the terrain. However, it is not clear whether it is a Japanese warship or a warship of another country because its actions are erratic. We will continue to investigate. According to Wu Fengsheng, the magistrate of Xinhui County, on the 29th of last month, a British twin-chimney gunboat sailed to the Yamen sea and anchored. Two electric boats came with it, carrying two Westerners and dozens of Chinese, measuring the coast along Yangguan, Shangxia Sha, Jiaobeishi, Luohuan, Dahu, and Erhu. They also erected small black and white flags as markers. The ship sailed away on the evening of the 1st of this month. When customs officers questioned the British ship's crew, they replied that they had measured the water depth here more than ten years ago, and because it had been so long, they had come to measure it again. After receiving the report, the military authorities, considering that foreign relations are currently urgent and that British and Japanese warships have successively come to the sea frontiers to secretly measure the terrain and waterlines in the important sea forts, which has significant implications internationally, have instructed the county magistrates to investigate and prevent them at any time. They have also sent a telegram to Navy Commander Chen Ce, requesting him to dispatch a ship to remove all the small flags erected by foreigners. After receiving the telegram, the Navy Headquarters dispatched the Zhongshan ship on the 11th to handle the matter accordingly. (December 14)

鄂綏靖署卽成立

▲陳光組赴京請示已返漢覆命

▲第四師全部扺漢將協助剿匪

Hankou Correspondence: The reorganization of the E' provincial pacification headquarters from the Hankou military affairs headquarters has been rumored for a long time. However, due to the fact that the new organizational law has not yet been promulgated, the establishment has been delayed. He Chengjun believes that banditry has resurfaced in various counties of the E' province, especially in the Xiang River area, which is a haven for thieves. In order to eliminate them as soon as possible, the pacification headquarters should be established to command the various armies to be responsible for suppressing them. He specifically planned to go to Beijing on the 16th to visit Jiang for instructions in order to start the organization. Just as he was preparing his luggage, Jiang's telegram of resignation arrived in Hankou, so he suspended his trip and sent Chen Guangzu, the chief advisor of the military affairs headquarters, as his representative. Chen took a plane to Beijing on the 16th and returned to Hankou on the 18th. The organizational law of the pacification headquarters was also promulgated at the same time. He then decided to formally abolish the military affairs headquarters within a few days and establish the pacification headquarters. The content of the organization and internal expenses will be reduced to 15,000 yuan per month, so it is simpler than the military affairs headquarters. The personnel from various departments will also be transferred from the military affairs headquarters. As for the troops responsible for pacification, in addition to the original armies stationed in E', the 4th Division and the 83rd Division will also be transferred to E' to assist. The entire 4th Division, led by Division Commander Xu Tingyao, recently arrived in Hankou from Bian. It is said that the 83rd Division will also continue to arrive. After that, the military strength will be greater, and it will be easier to suppress the bandits. (December 18)

閩黨政軍會勘烟苗

▲漳泉各地烟苗甚盛

Fuzhou Correspondence: The Fujian Provincial Government sent a telegram to the Central Government requesting that senior officials be sent to Fujian to investigate the opium seedlings. The report has already been reported. However, the fact that opium is being planted in Fujian has become an undeniable reality. In Zhangzhou, where the planting was first started, the opium is about to be harvested. In Quanzhou and Xinghua, the opium seedlings have emerged to about one foot in height. Even in Funing, where the planting was last started, the seedlings have sprouted. Even in the southern district of the provincial capital, planting has begun. Therefore, the Provincial Government has decided to divide the province into four districts according to the investigation methods of last year: Funing as the first district, Xinghua as the second district, Quanzhou as the third district, and Zhangzhou as the fourth district. Two officials from the Provincial Government, the Provincial Party Department, and the Security Department, as well as one member of the Marine Corps and one member of the 49th Division, will be divided into two groups. Each group will have one member from the Provincial Government, the Provincial Party Department, and the Security Department. The first and second districts will be investigated by personnel from the 49th Division, and the third and fourth districts will be investigated by personnel from the Marine Corps. The Provincial Government has also sent a letter to the Party Department and the military, requesting them to designate personnel as soon as possible so that they can depart on time. These committee members have the power to dispatch troops to eradicate opium seedlings in the designated areas, but it is not known whether they will be able to do so thoroughly. Also, the Anti-Opium Support Association of all sectors of the provincial capital convened a meeting of various groups on the 14th at the County Party Department and resolved: (1) Please the Provincial Party Department to order the Party Departments of various counties to organize Anti-Opium Support Associations to lead the people to oppose opium planting. (2) For the protection of opium planting by the garrison troops, if they are national defense troops, please ask the Ministry of Military Affairs to deal with them severely. If they are provincial defense troops, please ask the Provincial Government to deal with them severely. If they are Marine Corps, please ask the Navy Department to deal with them severely. (3) Please ask the Provincial Government to dismiss and severely punish county magistrates who conceal opium seedlings in their counties. (4) Please ask the Provincial Government to implement effective opium prohibition measures. (December 15)

Jinpu Railway Traffic Interrupted Again

▲ Large Group of Students Gathering in Yanzhou

▲ Railway Bureau Forbids Carrying Students to Beijing

Jinan Dispatch: Students from various schools in Yanzhou, Jining, Caozhou, Tai'an, and Qufu are gathering in Yanzhou to petition in Beijing. Yesterday (the 16th), the southbound train No. 201 on the Pingpu line reached Tai'an. Over two hundred students from the Third Tai'an Middle School and the County Normal School forced their way onto the train. When the train arrived in Yanzhou, students gathered at the Yanzhou station and forced all passengers off the train so they could board. The station, having received prior orders not to transport students to Beijing, immediately telegraphed a report to the Jinan Railway Affairs Section. The section chief, Fang Bolin, both telegraphed the Railway Bureau for instructions and went to the provincial government to meet with Han Fuqu to discuss solutions. The provincial government immediately telegraphed the leading officials of various agencies in Yanzhou to go to the station and dissuade the students. The students remained resolute and refused to listen. As of this morning, the train has still not departed, and the stationmaster has absconded. The Jinpu Railway Affairs Office issued a public notice at 1:00 AM today, ordering southbound trains to temporarily travel only as far as Tai'an and northbound trains to temporarily travel only as far as Tengxian, awaiting further instructions before proceeding. As a result, both the southbound train No. 201 and the northbound train No. 2 complied with these orders this morning, and Jinpu Railway traffic has been interrupted once again. Travelers heading to Beijing from Pingjin are lamenting endlessly, with some disembarking in Jinan. This morning, Jinpu Railway Affairs Section Chief Fang Bolin received another telegram from the Railway Bureau reiterating the prohibition against transporting students to Beijing. Fang is currently taking the telegram to the provincial government to meet with Han and discuss solutions. The outcome remains unknown.

According to a report received by the Education Department from Zhao Derou, the principal of the Fourth Rural Normal School in Yanzhou, the students gathered in Yanzhou include those from the Third Tai'an Middle School, the County Normal School, the Third Vocational School in Yanzhou (only three students from that school), the Fourth Rural Normal School, the Second Normal School in Qufu, the Private Mingde Middle School, and the Seventh Middle School in Jining, totaling about one thousand students. Additionally, Xu Meisheng, the principal of the Fifth Middle School in Linyi, also telegraphed the Education Department reporting that the entire student body of his school had also resolved to petition in Beijing, were fully prepared to depart, and were not heeding any dissuasion. As the school is in Linyi, which is not connected by train, they will either travel by car or on foot, likely gathering in Zaozhuang before boarding a train south. (17th)

A Portion of Japan's Illegal Pending Cases (5)

▲ Conflict Between Japanese Soldiers and Police in Tieling: Unauthorized Arrest and Humiliation of the Security Team Case On September 30 of the 18th year, a conflict occurred between Japanese soldiers in Tieling County and soldiers from the county's security team due to a minor argument. The Japanese soldiers retreated and assembled a force of over one hundred soldiers, surrounding the security team's headquarters. Both sides of the main street were filled with their formations. The security team tightly closed its doors. Just as the director of the negotiation bureau and the section chief of the county government, together with the chief of the Japanese police station, arrived to investigate, the Japanese consul and the commander of the Japanese army regiment also arrived. While they were in the midst of discussions, the director of the negotiation bureau went to find the head of the public security bureau to be responsible for maintaining order. The Japanese soldiers took the opportunity to pry open the main gate and stormed into the headquarters, disarming the security soldiers and ordering them, along with nearby merchants who were also detained, to kneel on the ground, subjecting them to all kinds of humiliation. Before leaving, they tied up over thirty officers and soldiers, seized numerous firearms and bullets, and destroyed the equipment of several families nearby, including Yang Juqi's, looting their clothing and decorations. The detained soldiers suffered severe torture. After negotiations, the soldiers and firearms were gradually returned. The negotiation bureau, based on the seven conditions proposed by the county government, negotiated with the Japanese side for punishment of the perpetrators, compensation, apologies, guarantees, and assurances that Japanese soldiers would not enter the interior armed without notifying and receiving permission from the Chinese side in the future. A satisfactory resolution has yet to be reached.

▲ Fuzhou Japanese Merchants' and Taiwanese Residents' Perpetual Lease Land Tax Deed Case Japanese merchants and residents of Taiwanese origin in Fuzhou only register their business addresses with the Japanese consulate and do not follow formal procedures by submitting their deeds to the Chinese authorities for verification and tax stamping. Among them, Taiwanese residents account for eighty or ninety percent, often leading to disputes over property rights. The former Fujian Negotiation Office repeatedly sent letters to the Japanese consul stationed in Fuzhou between October and December of the 18th year, requesting that he instruct Japanese residents to submit their deeds to the Chinese authorities for verification and tax stamping in accordance with past practices, and declaring that if they failed to comply, the Chinese authorities would not recognize any future disputes. However, Japanese residents have consistently refused to comply. In February of the 20th year, the Chinese side brought this matter up in negotiations with the Japanese ambassador, who claimed that the Japanese government had never recognized this procedure and should not forcibly enforce it on Japanese residents. The Chinese side discovered that British, American, and other foreign merchants in Fuzhou, as well as churches in the interior, have always submitted their deeds to the Chinese authorities for verification and tax stamping for all their perpetually leased land and buildings, without exception. On the Japanese side, the Bank of Taiwan, the Japanese Residents' Association, and the Bo'ai Hospital have also complied with the aforementioned procedures. Therefore, the Japanese ambassador's claim that this procedure had never been recognized is untrue. In May of the same year, a letter was sent to the Japanese ambassador requesting that he instruct Japanese residents to comply, but no reply has been received.

▲ Killing of a Fanyang Farmer by Japanese Soldiers Case On October 17 of the 18th year, a farmer from Shenyang was shot and killed by Japanese guards while passing by the side of the South Manchuria Railway. After an investigation by the local authorities and discussions, the Japanese guards claimed that they were within their guard zone and had the right to exercise their guard duties, and therefore were not responsible. The Fujian Farmers' Association submitted a report to the central government, which forwarded it to the Ministry of Foreign Affairs, requesting that the Liaoning Provincial Government earnestly negotiate. However, they have yet to comply.

▲ Yanji Japanese Police Surround a Branch Office of the Xilin River Self-Defense Corps and Arrest a Teacher Case At 4:00 PM on January 13 of the 19th year, Takeda Hakuji, an assistant police inspector from the Japanese consulate branch in Toutaogou, suddenly led twenty-one armed Japanese police officers and surrounded the Xilin River Self-Defense Corps branch office, claiming they needed to speak with Han Xingli, a reclaimed land resident from the Eleventh School (the school and the branch office were located in the same courtyard). While the school principal and the team leader were inside the office negotiating with him, the Japanese police outside enticed Teacher Han out and took him away. The Toutaogou Commercial Port Branch Bureau negotiated with the Japanese consulate branch, which claimed that they were acting on orders from the consul-general and had already taken him to Longjing Village. The special envoy from Jilin negotiated with the Japanese consul-general for his release, demanding punishment, apologies, and guarantees, among other conditions. The Ministry of Foreign Affairs also sent a letter to the Japanese ambassador requesting that he instruct them to comply. The Japanese ambassador replied that the matter had been discussed and resolved satisfactorily between the director of the Yanji Municipal Preparatory Office and the Japanese consul-general. However, according to a report from the Jilin envoy cited by the Ministry of Foreign Affairs, Han Xingli had not returned to school. After repeated urging, the Japanese ambassador was instructed to handle the matter swiftly, but no reply has been received.

Case of the Japanese Ship Toyomaru Smuggling Military Supplies On February 23 of the 19th year, the Japanese ship Toyomaru secretly transported military supplies into China, totaling one hundred and five boxes of firearms, ammunition, and medicine, which were seized by the Shidao Customs. Together with the local military police, they detained the Japanese national Fujita Tokichi and others, along with the military supplies. The Japanese consul stationed in Yantai requested that the Japanese nationals be guarded by the consulate. On March 8, the Japanese consul personally took them away, stating that he would be responsible for returning them and guaranteeing that the Toyomaru would not leave the port. The next day, the Japanese warship Kusaki led the Toyomaru out of the port. After negotiations with the Japanese consul, he replied that the ship had been damaged while unloading the military supplies, so he had ordered it to sail to Dalian for repairs. The Chinese side sent a letter to the Japanese ambassador, requesting that he instruct the Japanese consul in Yantai to return the Toyomaru and its crew for legal proceedings. The ambassador replied that the Toyomaru's departure for Dalian for repairs at the time coincided with the Japanese warship's return to Lushun for Army Memorial Day, which was a misunderstanding. He also stated that evidence had been collected from the Yantai Qingdao Kwantung Leased Territory regarding the perpetrators in this case, and a strict trial was being conducted.

▲ Case of Yanji Japanese Police Arresting Jin Rensan, Deputy Chairman of the Farmers' Association Jin Rensan, the deputy chairman of the Shangyi Township Farmers' Association in Yanji, was arrested by Japanese police and sent to the Japanese consulate on April 30 of the 19th year. Prior to this, on April 13, Japanese police arrested over twenty students in Longjing Village. On April 14, they arrested Li Yuanshi, the head of the first section, in Toutaogou, and arrested over fifty teachers and students from a reclaimed land school and section head Jin in Xiaowudaogou, as well as Yang Taixi and others from Beigou reclaimed land. The Yanji Municipal Preparatory Office and the Longjing Village Commercial Port Bureau repeatedly protested and negotiated with the Japanese side, but the Japanese side always used forceful arguments and refused to comply. The Yanji Municipal Preparatory Office then sent a letter through the Jilin Special Envoy, which was approved by the Ministry of Foreign Affairs, to protest to the Japanese ambassador, requesting that he instruct the local Japanese consul to release all of them immediately, but no reply has been received to date. (To be continued)

Local Correspondence

Songjiang

Tragedy Caused by Showing a Movie According to those coming to Shanghai from Songjiang, there is a Songwei Long-Distance Station building at the Malu Bridge in Songjiang. The Yuying Primary School borrowed the building to show movies and host various recreational activities to raise funds. It was originally scheduled for ten days. The seventeenth evening was the third day. The garrison troops in Songcheng sent inspection teams in shifts to check the premises. On that evening, seven military police were present first. When the tax police entered, they were refused entry by the military police and left. After returning to their unit, the tax police gathered many of their brothers, initially planning to question the military police. Seeing a large group of armed soldiers arriving, the movie theater closed its iron gates. The tax police could not enter, leading to a standoff. The situation became extremely tense in an instant. Both sides opened fire. Platoon Leader Li of the tax police pleaded on his knees, but he was shot and killed on the spot. Another tax policeman was also shot and killed on the spot. When the two sides clashed, the audience, including men, women, children, and the elderly, cried and screamed loudly. After the gunfire started, everyone lay on the ground. Fortunately, various agencies heard the alarm and rushed to the scene to suppress the situation, allowing the civilians in the theater to be released first. Then, the officers ordered everyone to return to their respective units. (18th) The deceased have already been collected by personnel dispatched from the County Court for an autopsy.

Nanhui

Tenth District Chief Resigns Due to Boundary Dispute Wang Yingyi, the district chief of the Tenth District of this county, resigned yesterday after a dispute arose over the proposed merger of Taiping and other townships into Fengxian, resulting in the destruction of the district office. The county government approved his resignation and temporarily appointed Zhang Jin'ou, the district chief of the Fifth District, to serve concurrently.

Murder of Husband by Wife and Lover in the Fifth District Qu Gensheng, who ran a small shop in Tangjiao Village, Nicheng, in the Fifth District, had a wife, Hu, who was secretly having an affair with Hu Xianglou. Their passion was intense. Yesterday at twelve o'clock, Hu Xianglou and Hu took advantage of Qu's deep sleep to strangle him. Qu cried out for help, which was heard by Zhang Guichun, a neighbor, who rushed to investigate. He encountered Hu Xianglou hurrying out, looking panicked. Zhang immediately grabbed him and entered the house, where he found Qu strangled to death. He immediately handed Hu Xianglou over to the Nicheng Public Security Bureau that night, who, together with the Fifth District Office, sent him to the county for questioning.

Discovery of Hermaphrodite Female Prisoner The Zhangjiang Defense Regiment arrested eight suspects the day before yesterday, including a female prisoner named Zhu A'bao. After interrogation by the county court, she was ordered to be released on bail. However, because she was from out of town, no one was willing to bail her out, so she was temporarily detained in the women's prison. Today, the prison guard reported that although Zhu A'bao is female, she is actually deformed, with male genitalia clearly visible (commonly known as a hermaphrodite), causing the other female prisoners in the same cell to be afraid to share a room with her. They requested instructions on how to handle the situation. Upon receiving the report, the county government immediately made arrangements to guard her separately.

Wuxi

Complete Reorganization of the Anti-Japanese Association The various Anti-Japanese National Salvation Associations were initially jointly organized by representatives from various groups, but were later controlled by a small number of people, leading to unhealthy work practices and extreme corruption. After a joint meeting of the various district Anti-Japanese Associations, it was decided to send a letter requiring that the accounts be published within three days and that the fines paid by various businesses be investigated for verification. The County Anti-Japanese Association also found its work difficult, and all the committee members submitted their resignations to the County Party Headquarters yesterday. The County Party Headquarters approved this, immediately sending personnel to take over and ordering various groups to re-nominate representatives in accordance with the organizational methods promulgated by the province for a complete reorganization. In addition, the registration fees of four percent paid by various industries totaled over 4,280 yuan, which was also decided to be allocated as follows: over 1,700 yuan to the Volunteer Army, over 850 yuan to the Social Boy Scouts, and over 1,700 yuan remaining, to be deposited in the Bank of China and the Bank of Communications for handover.

The County Executive Committee Continues to Work The County Executive Committee issued a notice yesterday, stating that the committee's work had never been interrupted. The emergence of the so-called Party Affairs Improvement Association had caused outsiders to misunderstand the situation, not knowing the underlying reasons. The notice stated that changes in Party affairs must be determined by the central government's improvement policy before the committee could dare to abandon its responsibilities without being formally reorganized by the provincial committee. The notice was issued in a solemn announcement, and the 43rd committee meeting was convened, with the following agenda: (1) Supporting the Fourth Plenary Session of the Central Committee; (2) Expressing a welcome to the Guangdong committee members traveling to Beijing; (3) Supporting Mr. Wang Jingwei's early arrival in Beijing to preside over the affairs of the Party and the country; (4) Committee members of the Anti-Japanese National Salvation Association resigning; =, ordering various groups to re-nominate representatives for a complete reorganization; (5) Scheduling an emergency meeting of all executive committee members from all districts and branches in the county on the 21st of this month to discuss the promotion of Party affairs; (6) Some party members in the county initiated the organization of a Party Affairs Improvement Association, and the committee should telegraph the Provincial Party Headquarters for verification. The Party Affairs Improvement Association also held a committee meeting yesterday and decided on the following: (1) To hold a representative conference on the 25th of this month; (2) To appoint Zhu Zuyin and Xu Chizi as representatives to the National Salvation Association Promotion Association; (3) To severely punish Ji Pu, a member of the County Executive Committee, and Wang Ciqing and their supporters.

Kidnapping Case in the Sixteenth District Qian Quanrong, the owner of the Qian Yongmao Grain Shop in Yangshuyuan Town, Sixteenth District (Wan'an City), who is over forty years old and has a small amount of farmland, took a farmhand to the countryside to collect rent the day before yesterday. Unexpectedly, when they reached the Luoluo area of Kuangqiao, a black awning boat appeared, and three burly men jumped out and blocked their path. Seeing this, Qian and his servant resisted the bandits, but they were outnumbered. As a result, Qian and his farmhand were both kidnapped onto the bandits' boat, which sped away. Yesterday, the incident was reported to the local Public Security Bureau and the Commercial Corps for investigation.

Nantong

Higher Court Sends Commissioner to Investigate Opium Burning Scandal In Nantong County, irregularities were discovered in the burning of opium, involving over one thousand taels of opium. The Higher Court sent Commissioner Shen Yuan to Nantong, and on the 18th, he convened a meeting of representatives from various sectors at the County Court to solicit opinions for a thorough investigation. However, the representatives present noted that the opium packages, which had been sealed in public days earlier, had been opened, and raised questions about responsibility. Commissioner Shen returned to Suzhou to request instructions.

Cracks Appear in Nantong's Financial Circles The financial situation in Nantong has been unusually tight recently. After the collapse of the Housheng Pawnshop, the Yongchang Lin Zhuang, a major player in the money industry, also collapsed on the 18th. Several other businesses have also run aground due to a lack of liquidity.

All Middle Schools and Above in the County Stage a Strike and Demonstration Students from all middle schools and above in Nantong County went on strike on the 18th, gathering at the public sports field for a demonstration.

Jiangyin

Activities After the Middle School Strike Following the order from the Provincial Student Anti-Japanese National Salvation Association, Jiangyin Middle Schools held a general strike on the 17th. However, the County Middle School continued to hold classes. Xu Juexin and others from the school's student union committee requested instructions from Gao Qingyue, the chairman of the student federation. Gao replied that if they did not strike on the 18th, they should request instructions from the Provincial Student Association. In the afternoon, the Anti-Japanese Executive Committee, the Discipline Committee, and the Autonomous Court of the Nanzhaung district held a meeting and passed resolutions regarding the active Anti-Japanese National Salvation affairs during the strike period by executive committee members. The discipline committee would execute all disciplinary matters. The autonomous court would execute all internal dispute-related rulings.

Rickshaw Operators Oppose the Construction Bureau's Harsh Levies The Construction Bureau, due to the collapse of roads in the urban area, estimated the cost of repairs to be quite high. It planned to charge a registration fee of five yuan per rickshaw to fund the work. More than twenty rickshaw companies, using a monthly contribution of one yuan and three cents per vehicle based on 200 vehicles (80 vehicles added this year are not yet included), would contribute 260 yuan per month. This was a road maintenance fee, calculated from September of the 18th year to the present, a total of twenty-eight months. They are very unwilling to pay the registration fee, since it adds up to a substantial amount of 7,280 yuan. They presented their case to both the Party and the government, requesting that the Construction Bureau settle the accounts for road maintenance.

Qingjiang

Robbery and Arson Seen Again in the Southern Countryside The families of Liu Dianrong and Zhang Xuedao outside the South Gate of Huaiyin, among others, were previously subjected to arson and robbery by bandits, with as many as seven or eight people killed or injured. Now, at one o'clock on the night of the 10th, over thirty bandits, each carrying sharp weapons, arrived at Gujiazhuang, located at the junction of Huaiyin and Huai'an counties near Taiping Bridge in the southern countryside. They first burned down the house of Gu Zhibang and abducted Zhibang's eldest son. Then, they searched and looted nearby houses, abducting six men and women. All of the village's livestock, clothing, and other belongings were stolen.

The Prison Administration Offers Rewards for Apprehending Escaped Prisoners On the evening of November 7, three prisoners from the Huaiyin Prison, Qian Xuelun, Wan Shiyou (life imprisonment), and Hu Daizi (ten years' imprisonment), escaped from prison by tunneling through a wall. Subsequent searches have yielded no traces. Now that more than a month has passed, there is still no progress.

Therefore, the reward amount has been increased, and rewards are offered for their capture.

Jiaxing

Smashing a Bandit Den and Rescuing a Hostage The Jiaxing Chamber of Commerce Volunteer Security Regiment, having learned that a bandit den was located in the eastern part of the city, dispatched Vice Squad Leader Hu Fei Qian and other members on the night of the 17th. They arrived at No. 38 on the south side of the Weicheng branch factory near Yancang Bridge, where the door was ajar. They immediately barged in, capturing Chen A'da, a Taizhou native guarding the hostage, as well as Zhu Zhushi, the sister of Zhu A'er. They also found Chen Jikang (12 years old), the son of Chen Lida, a farmer from Yuxian Township, in a secret room. He had been kidnapped on the seventh day of the eighth lunar month while returning home from Yuxian Primary School. Because his family was poor and unable to pay the ransom, they took the group of people back to the First Squad Headquarters. Later, the Nanyan Police Station arrested Shangshi, the mother of Zhu A'er. The squad also arrested Chen Ruan, the wife of the bandit leader Chen, in Juren Lane in front of the Xuanmiao Temple. According to her confession, Zhu A'er was also involved and was working as a foreman on the Pinghu to Xincang shuttle boat. The squad headquarters immediately notified the Pinghu Patrol Brigade to arrest him. On the 18th, the group of people was sent to the joint military and police office for processing. The hostage was left at the squad headquarters, and the family was notified to come to He City to claim him.

Hangzhou

Citywide Students Raise National Salvation Funds The Hangzhou City Secondary School and Above Student Anti-Japanese National Salvation United Association decided at a meeting to launch a fund-raising campaign for national salvation on the 19th and 20th. More than twenty schools participated in the fundraising, collecting donation receipts and bamboo tubes from the United Association, and then departing to raise funds. They also took highway buses to Jianggan, Zhakou, Gongchen Bridge, and other places to raise funds, so that they could deposit the money in banks and use it as national salvation funds.

Zhang Nanxian Departs for Beijing Zhang Nanxian, the former chairman of the Zhejiang Provincial Government, was relieved of his duties after the national government issued a reorganization order. Zhang had visited the scenic Mogan Mountain and handed over his responsibilities to the new chairman, Lu, at the provincial government on the 18th. At 12:00 PM, he gathered all the staff of the various departments to say goodbye, then returned to his private residence. At 9:50 AM this morning, Zhang, accompanied by a servant and carrying light luggage, took the thirty-first express train to Beijing to report everything to the central government.

Ningbo

Bandits Set Fire, Loot, and Kill In Hutan Village, located at the border of Fenghua and Sheng counties, and inhabited by more than fifty families, over a hundred bandits suddenly arrived last night. They first surrounded the Security Corps, who, being outnumbered, fled. The bandits did not pursue them, but instead engaged in widespread arson and looting. After an investigation, it was found that one member of the Security Corps and over ten villagers, both men and women, had been shot and killed, and that about seven-tenths of the village's houses had been burned down, resulting in losses of tens of thousands of gold, a veritable disaster.

Bride Kidnapped Tang, a wealthy resident of Jiangkouwan Dapo, Siming Township, located at the border of Yuyao and Shangyu counties, had two sons. His second son was working as a clerk at a money shop in Ningbo. He got married at his home on the evening of the 14th of this month. Unexpectedly, as the bride arrived home and was about to perform the wedding ceremony, a number of bandits suddenly arrived. They first kidnapped the bride and then ransacked the house, stealing over one thousand yuan worth of cash, clothing, and other items.

Over Five Hundred Fishing Boats Overturned in a Storm According to reliable sources in the fishing industry, on the afternoon of the 11th of this month at around 8:00 PM, fishing boats from various places gathered in the sea area of Haijiao, located at the border of Jiangsu and Zhejiang provinces, to fish. Suddenly, a violent storm struck, overturning over five hundred large and small fishing boats and killing or injuring over one thousand fishermen.

Xiaoshan

The Devastation of the Ding Family in Xianghu In recent days, theft cases have occurred frequently in the four villages of Xiaoshan. On the night of the 15th, over twenty bandits suddenly arrived at the house of Ding Huanzhang, a kiln operator in Xianghu, carrying firearms and knives. They broke through the surrounding wall and entered, then went upstairs and engaged in widespread looting. They stole over twenty gold rings, 280 pearls, over 150 yuan in silver dollars, nine leather jackets, and two large boxes of silk, satin, and clothing, resulting in losses worth over two thousand yuan. They also injured two women in the family. After an hour, they fired a warning shot and fled west.

County Magistrate Visits the Western Townships to Survey Boundary Lines Xiaoshan and Hang County are adjacent to the Qiantang sandbar. Due to the boundary relationship, the provincial government repeatedly ordered surveys and divisions, but a clear division has not been achieved. Taking advantage of his inspection of the townships, County Magistrate Lin, accompanied by the district chief, met at Wenyan on the 17th to jointly survey and implement the boundary division.

Education News

Special Feature: The Three Principles of the People and University Education (Cont. 2) - Zheng Hongnian

(C) Vocational Training and Construction

The primary task of construction is to address the people's livelihood, the four basic necessities of clothing, food, housing, and transportation. Even the most trivial aspects require the application of scientific methods. Therefore, university students must emphasize practical science, and schools should enrich their curriculum and focus on vocational training. The goal is to cultivate specialized talent with knowledge and skills to serve the nation and society. Currently, the nation is in crisis. University students are rallying and striving to be leaders of society and the people. Their passionate enthusiasm is truly commendable. However, Mr. Hu Hanmin said, "Do not merely vent your emotions, but cultivate your strength." The conflict between China and Japan cannot be resolved overnight. In the past, Denmark was defeated by Germany, ceded territory, and paid indemnities. The nation's strength was depleted, and it was on the verge of collapse. The people's hearts were scattered, their spirits were low, and industry and commerce were underdeveloped. Its situation was arguably worse than China's today. However, thanks to the efforts and leadership of the educator Grundtvig, the nation was revived. Denmark was primarily an agricultural country, and Grundtvig established a folk high school in the countryside. All young people aged eighteen to thirty received this education, which developed agriculture and increased the nation's wealth. He also promoted agricultural cooperation to stabilize society and eliminate labor-management disputes. In less than fifty years, Denmark became one of the most stable and prosperous nations in the world. China's production is backward, its science is underdeveloped, and it faces internal and external troubles. The lessons of history are not far off. It is hoped that outstanding young people receiving higher education will thoroughly engage in scientific research, receive vocational training, build a new China based on the Three Principles of the People, complete the National Revolution, and promote universal harmony.

4. Conclusion

The degree of world evolution always depends on the speed of academic competition. Since the Three Principles of the People contain all academic disciplines, the development of academics can reveal the progress of the Three Principles of the People's construction. The development of science has varying speeds, which means that the construction of the Three Principles of the People also has priorities. As the saying goes, "Things have roots and branches, and events have beginnings and ends. Knowing what comes first and what comes last is the path to understanding." "The way of great learning consists in manifesting clear virtue, renovating the people, and resting in the highest excellence." Achieving the realm of ultimate goodness creates a center of social ethics. Confucius once lamented, "I have not been able to see a good person. If I could see someone with perseverance, that would be acceptable. To lack and pretend to have, to be empty and pretend to be full, to be constrained and pretend to be grand – it is difficult to have perseverance. Perseverance is the gateway to virtue." This shows that achieving virtue always begins with perseverance. He listed three examples of vain boasting to warn those who cannot maintain constancy. He also said, "If a good person governs a state for a hundred years, they can overcome cruelty and eliminate killing." Alas, the world is now in turmoil, with endless cruelty and killing. Where can we find a good person to govern the state and save the people from suffering? The purpose of university education is to create a center of social ethics that rests in ultimate goodness. University education under the leadership of the Three Principles of the People aims to cultivate virtuous individuals who can govern the state for a hundred years (End).

Important News

No Confucius Shrine Can Be Set Up in Schools

▲Reply from the Ministries of Interior and Education to the Central Committee

The Secretariat of the Central Executive Committee previously sent a letter to the Ministries of Interior and Education, stating that the Standing Committee had forwarded a report from the Hunan Provincial Party Guidance Committee regarding a request from the Chen County Executive Committee to confirm the status of hanging Sun Yat-sen's portrait and posting Confucius' shrine in schools. It was approved that the matter concerned education and etiquette and should be submitted to the Ministries of Education and Interior for proper verification and reply. The Ministries of Interior and Education have now jointly replied to the Secretariat of the Central Executive Committee with the results of their discussion of the case, stating that they had approved the public letter from your office regarding the approved forwarding of the Hunan Provincial Party Committee's request to confirm the hanging of Sun Yat-sen's portrait and the posting of Confucius' shrine in schools. They are specially sending this letter to inform you of the verification and reply, along with a copy of the original report. They have found that there is no legal basis for posting Confucius' shrine in schools. If Confucius is considered a religious leader, it would violate the legal provision that "no religious ceremonies may be held in schools." Even for Confucius' birthday commemoration, there is no need to set up a Confucius shrine in schools. The reply is being sent as requested. Please inform your office to verify and report. Furthermore, this case was drafted by the Ministry of Education, which also makes this statement.

He Jian Convenes School Principals for Talks

▲Hoping to Broaden Their Vision to the "Question of China's Survival"

(Changsha Correspondence) He Jian has returned from Nanjing and Shanghai, believing that the student patriotic movement is extremely important. He believes that most Chinese people are spiritually dead, but young students are still energetic. However, he fears that their objectives are unclear, their steps are not unified, and they are easily exploited by others. Therefore, on the 16th of this month, he convened principals, deans of discipline, deans of academics, and directors of military training from secondary schools and above throughout the province to the provincial government for talks. Xie Zuyou, Zhu Haohuai, and Huang Jiasheng from the Provincial Party Committee; Cao Dianqiu, a member of the Provincial Government; Cao Bowen, Zhang Kailian, Huang Shiheng, and Tan Changkai, the directors of the four departments of civil affairs, finance, education, and construction; Chen Changzu, the president of the High Court; and Yao Xuehuai, Huang Baoxuan, and Huang Ji from the Municipal Party Committee, totaling over a hundred people, attended. After refreshments, He Jian stood up to give a long speech. The main points were: first, he described the recent situation in various parts of the country; second, he described the recent conspiracy of the Red bandits to harm the Party and the country during the national crisis. Therefore, while advocating for resistance against Japan and national salvation, it is also necessary to pay attention to suppressing the Reds. He then mentioned that the Hunan education community's past leadership of the patriotic movement of young people was very orderly and praised by people everywhere. He said that young people are the backbone of the national salvation movement, and he hoped that the education community would broaden their vision to the "question of China's survival" and lead young people to truly save the country. He also listed the points that teachers should pay attention to regarding students and the responsibilities they should bear towards the country, society, students' parents, and the students themselves. He explained in great detail. Finally, he explained his sincerity in wanting to improve Hunan and hoped that all sectors of the Party, government, military, and academia would unite to overcome the national crisis. Tan Changkai from the Provincial Party Committee, Zhang Kailian from the Finance Department, Yao Xuehuai and Huang Baoxuan from the Municipal Party Committee, and Cao Mu from the Military Training Department of Hunan University also spoke, mostly expressing their hope that from now on, everyone would unite to save Hunan and save China.

A Letter to All Sectors from Professors of the College of Engineering, Zhejiang University

▲Regarding the Demonstration Movement by Students from Various Schools in Hangzhou on December 10th

A Letter to All Sectors from All Professors of the College of Engineering, National Zhejiang University:

We have been hired to fill these positions and hope to contribute our humble knowledge to assist students in studying and researching science to save China, which is lagging behind in science. Since taking office, we have been busy day and night, immersed in lecturing, experiments, reference materials, and research. Fortunately, the students are diligent in their studies, and their scientific knowledge has gradually increased. The College of Engineering of Zhejiang University has a good reputation in society. We hope to continue this progress and join the ranks of renowned universities around the world. However, since the September 18th Incident, when the violent Japanese invaded, the students, filled with righteous indignation, organized an Anti-Japanese National Salvation Association and formed a Student Volunteer Army to carry out their patriotic movement. This is the natural duty of a citizen, and we deeply support it. We have all participated in the organization of the Anti-Japanese National Salvation Association and the training of the Volunteer Army. Later, when the Zhejiang Provincial Party Headquarters established the Hangzhou City Anti-Japanese National Salvation United Association, our college also joined as a member. At that time, the inspectors of Japanese goods hired by the United Association often failed to fulfill their responsibilities. Students from various schools were repeatedly called upon to inspect in groups. Our students worked tirelessly, braving wind and rain, taking turns to go out, and performing their duties conscientiously, which was highly valued by the Party Headquarters. As a result, they received written and verbal orders to mobilize most of our students to be responsible for searching Gao Yitai's private collection of Japanese goods. The students followed the locations listed in the written order and were led by a special envoy. They successfully seized a large amount of Japanese goods and, fearing that they would be secretly moved, guarded them overnight, without food or drink, in order to thoroughly handle the matter and deter others. Later, the United Association delayed the case for many days and eventually settled it vaguely with a fine of 6,000 yuan. The College of Engineering students could not understand the Party Headquarters' excuses to various parties and suspected the corruption of the United Association's personnel. They also believed that students joined the United Association not to help it but to be exploited by it as a tool. They gradually lost faith in the Party Headquarters. When students from various schools in Hangzhou planned to form another Student Anti-Japanese National Salvation United Association, the College of Engineering students also joined and planned to join the various sectors Anti-Japanese United Association in the name of the Student Federation Anti-Japanese Association, following the example of Shanghai and Nanjing. However, the Party Headquarters did not recognize this organization and issued a notice through the Education Department to ban it, leading to the December 10th demonstration. They petitioned the Provincial Party Headquarters unsuccessfully, resulting in the beating of committee members, the smashing of objects, and a petition to the Education Department, which refused to meet with them, leading to damage to Director Zhang's private residence and belongings. We were unable to prevent this unexpected action beforehand, and we will share the responsibility for failing to educate them properly. However, the Provincial Party Headquarters issued a statement after the event, suspecting that President Li Zhenwu had condoned it and blaming it on the College of Engineering, as if the students from other schools were all coerced and deceived by the College of Engineering. This false propaganda is far from the truth and clearly serves another purpose. Recently, we also received a joint letter from the printing, transportation, and pharmaceutical workers' unions, claiming that the College of Engineering students were cutting off their livelihoods. Today, the various workers' unions have issued statements denying this, which shows that someone is fabricating facts with the intention of sabotage. We do not need to argue further. However, we cannot help but speak about the students' Anti-Japanese National Salvation and the organization of the Volunteer Army, which came from a sincere and patriotic mentality, open and selfless. The Party Headquarters' emphasis on the College of Engineering students and their assignment of the important task of searching Gao Yitai was also purely based on a serious and selfless mentality. At that time, the Hangzhou Minguo Daily repeatedly praised the College of Engineering students and encouraged them in every possible way. However, the College of Engineering students lost faith in the Party Headquarters due to the superficial handling of the Gao case, which led to this unfortunate incident. They took actions that harmed order out of a love for the country, which we deeply regret. The Provincial Party Headquarters praised the College of Engineering students before but now focuses on attacking the College of Engineering and blaming it on one school. The attitude is completely different, and we cannot understand the intention. We hold teaching positions at the college and are responsible for guiding and advising students. However, according to current laws and regulations, all mass organizations are guided by the Party Headquarters. Therefore, since the outbreak of this Anti-Japanese movement, we have only joined in our individual capacity and have fully trusted the Party Headquarters in guiding the students' actions, without expressing any opinions to avoid misunderstandings. Now that this unfortunate incident has occurred, we believe that while the students' actions may have exceeded the boundaries, the Party Headquarters also failed to fully fulfill its guiding responsibilities. At this time of national crisis, we dare not lag behind in our love for the country. We sincerely hope that both sides will repent for their past mistakes and work to make amends, moving towards the path of resisting Japan and saving the nation, rather than using divisive tactics to cause greater disputes. Furthermore, the College of Engineering has been established for over twenty years, and its graduates have served in all sectors, numbering thousands. The achievements of the school are well known to society. All teachers and students of the school are extremely protective of their alma mater and will fight with all their strength against any external sabotage. We respectfully ask for your understanding. Respectfully submitted by all professors of the College of Engineering, National Zhejiang University, December 15th, 1931.

Telegram to the Central Government from Professors of Hunan University

Telegram to the Central Government from Qian Weizong and others, professors of Hunan University: To Chairman Chiang, presented by Committee Member Shao Lizi, Hubu Street, Nanjing. China today can only defend after it can fight, and can only negotiate after it can defend. Fighting must be used as a means, and defense as the goal. Even if we lack the strength to fight, we must stand firm. We respectfully request that you issue a conscription order immediately and set a deadline for repairing coastal and river fortresses and batteries. In terms of strategy, commercial warfare is superior to military warfare. We also request that you issue a clear order to restrict the export of Japanese grain and raw materials and actively promote the establishment of domestic goods factories. The urgent telegram cannot wait. We are awaiting orders. Respectfully submitted by Wu Depei and Qian Weizong, professors of Hunan University.

The students from various places who went to Beijing to demonstrate were forced to return to their hometowns because they were interfered with by the Capital Garrison Headquarters and escorted back by the military police. The Shanghai student demonstration group also arrived in Shanghai at around 1:00 AM yesterday and returned to their respective schools. Yesterday, some of the students from major secondary schools in Shanghai who went to Beijing and went missing also returned to Shanghai. The details are recorded below.

▲Students Continue to Return: Many students who went missing in Beijing were scattered after the incident on the 17th. About seventy or eighty missing students who stayed in Beijing returned to Shanghai at 1:00 AM yesterday. However, yesterday afternoon, missing students from more than ten schools, including Fudan University and Shanghai Middle School, returned to Shanghai one after another.

▲Estimated Casualties: The number of student casualties in this incident is still being compiled in detail. According to a survey conducted by the New Voice Society of various schools, there were about twenty or so student deaths, about thirty injuries, and about sixty arrests. More than thirty of those arrested have been released, leaving about twenty. The largest number of missing people is about sixty. Xiangzhong had two deaths, Wensheng had one death, and Jinan, Fudan, Jiaotong University, and Xiangzhong had a total of more than twenty injuries. The students from Pingji and other places suffered less losses. Suzhou had the most missing people. The entire group that went to Beijing consisted of sixty people, but only six survived when they returned to Suzhou. There were hundreds of casualties, missing, and arrested people from various places. Detailed damage still needs to be investigated.

▲Representatives Investigate: The demonstration groups from various schools in Shanghai have returned to Shanghai, and each school has sent one representative to stay in Beijing to investigate the deaths and injuries of students from their respective schools. It will take three or four days to complete the investigation.

▲Report from the China Medical College: Many students from various places who went to Beijing to demonstrate were injured. According to a survey by the China Medical College Rescue Team, one student from Jiaotong University, two from Xiangzhong, three from Fudan, three from Shanghai Middle School (one of whom was only fifteen years old and was severely stabbed by a bayonet), five from Suzhou Middle School, one female student from Suzhou Women's Normal School (stabbed in the abdomen by a bayonet), and one student from Southeast Medical College (injured in the shoulder by a wooden stick and had their uniform torn) were injured. (Shanghai News Agency)

Pan Gongzhan Resigns as Vice-President of China Public School

Pan Gongzhan, the vice-president of China Public School, yesterday telegraphed Cai Yuanpei, the chairman of the board of directors, requesting permission to resign and announced in the newspaper that he would no longer be responsible. The announcement is excerpted below: In the spring of this year, Gongzhan was appointed as a director of China Public School. In early autumn, due to Mr. Zhu Jingnong's departure from Shanghai, the board of directors appointed Gongzhan as vice-president. The task was heavy, and he declined repeatedly, but he was unable to refuse. He believed that education was of utmost importance, and China Public School was a school with a history. At that time, President Shao happened to be traveling far away, and he could not bear to see it without a leader. Even with his busy schedule, he had to reluctantly take on the task to maintain the temporary situation. However, since the September 18th Incident, the whole country has been indignant. Gongzhan also guided students to organize groups and engage in Anti-Japanese National Salvation work. However, the student population is unusually complex. Recently, there have been disputes over the Anti-Japanese National Salvation Executive Committee, resulting in mutual beatings. As a result, there have been more absurd actions, such as supporting or rejecting certain individuals. National hatred has not been resisted, but fellow students are fighting each other. His guidance was ineffective, and he was extremely heartbroken. He immediately telegraphed Chairman Cai and President Shao, requesting permission to resign from the position of vice-president and to convene a board of directors meeting as soon as possible to discuss everything. In the meantime, he has temporarily handed over the school affairs to Dean Fan to handle jointly with the three presidents, Xie, Liu, and Ying, under the instructions of President Shao. This special announcement declares that he will no longer be responsible for the school affairs of China Public School from the date of this announcement. We hope you will take note of this announcement. December 20th, 1931.
