Free Talk

Random Thoughts on the Dark Horse

— Meng Die

Previously, this column saw Dong Jun using "dark horse" as a subtle antithesis. Wanting to praise General Zhan Shanyuan, Jiang Jun then used the words "red sheep" to pair it, which was very clever and apt. I think that the words "yellow dragon" can also be used to pair it, and "Directly attack the Yellow Dragon" is a heroic saying of Yue Wumu (Yue Fei), and also refers to northern affairs. Now that the violent sun is invading, the military men are as timid as rats, falling at the first sight. Only General Zhan Shan Yuan alone displays heroic might, fighting the many with the few, and repeatedly winning battles. Our country today is as weak as the Southern Song Dynasty, and the general's loyalty and bravery are reminiscent of Yue Wumu. Alas, a withered fruit, a lone star after dawn, a rooster crowing in the wind and rain, a crane in the vast sky. I regret that there are too few General Ma! Indeed, he is rare and valuable. Therefore, I use the words "dark horse, yellow ridge" to create a couplet to praise him: "Guarding the territory, demonstrating unwavering loyalty, the whole country admires the dark horse. Revenging and extending great ambitions, in the future, directly attack the Yellow Dragon." The general's talent is not only enough to defend himself. If the words "dark horse" are only used for literal antithesis, then any colored animal will do, which is an insentient antithesis, and the meaning is lost far away.

Don't Remove the Weeds in the Courtyard, Random Talks by Zhai Fu

Hold On

—

"Let's go buy some firecrackers to set off for a good time!"

"Why are you so happy?"

"Jiang is out of office, peaceful unification, Guangzhou is parading and setting off firecrackers, can't we also set off some firecrackers to celebrate?"

"Hold on a bit with the happiness! Our firecrackers still have to be kept for some time before they can be set off."

"What day do we have to keep the firecrackers until we can make peace!"

"When the disaster-stricken compatriots have enough food and clothing, the lost territories of the eastern provinces are completely restored, the people of the whole country truly become the masters of the Republic of China, and all the oppressed people of the world turn over and become free men, then we will be interested in setting off firecrackers to celebrate!"

Biographies of Generals Zhang and Nie

— Zheng Yimei

Since the Japanese invaders have encroached upon our China, the people of the country are filled with righteous indignation, and there is a great momentum of feeding the horses and sharpening the weapons, determined to fight to the death. And we, the scribes, are searching through old papers and books to praise the famous generals who annihilated the Japanese in the past, as a contribution to discussion. This boosts morale, killing two birds with one stone. Who says it is not appropriate? The Generals Zhang and Nie that I am writing about are rising stars of the Huai Army. Zhang's name is Gao Yuan, and Nie's name is Shicheng. Both demonstrated military prowess and made achievements in the Sino-Japanese War of 1894-1895, which cannot be buried. Zhang is known for his courage and strategy. In battle, he often led the soldiers on horseback, disregarding the flying bullets as if they were nothing. People called him Zhang Yuzi. Zhang also used this as his pseudonym. When Lushun was lost, Zhang was ordered by Li Hefei to assist. At that time, Zhang commanded eight battalions of the Guangwu, Songwu, and newly recruited Fu troops, known for their strength. However, Lushun had already fallen before he could set out. Therefore, he followed the imperial decree to join Song Qing in defending Qianma Ridge. When the Japanese army attacked, Zhang fought with them, killing thousands of enemies. The Japanese army was defeated and withdrew. Afterwards, Song Qing summoned Zhang to discuss military affairs. Zhang asked to attack the enemy together. Song was jealous of Zhang's outstanding performance and greater prestige than his own, as a defeated general. He refused, threatening him with danger. Zhang said with emotion, "Zhang Yuzi is not a weak insect. I would rather die in battle. Danger is not to be feared." Therefore, Song became more wary of him and ordered him to move his troops to defend Gaiping. Zhang knew that Gaiping was a dangerous place with no defenses. Song's action was to trap him. However, the military order could not be violated, so he followed it. Before long, tens of thousands of Japanese troops attacked. Zhang remained calm, waiting for the enemy to get close before firing a volley of bullets, killing three Japanese generals. Zhang knew that the Japanese army would launch a large-scale siege and asked Song for reinforcements. Song did not respond. The next day, the Japanese army surged in like a tide, with bullets like dense rain and fog obscuring the view. He sent another messenger to ask Song for assistance. Song was stationed in Ximu City but remained motionless. Zhang was isolated and fought hard day and night, exhausted and out of ammunition. Then, he used blades to attack. The Japanese army's corpses were scattered all over the field. In the end, he was outnumbered and lost his commanders Li Shihong, Li Rendang, Yang Shoushan, Zhang Shibao, and Jia Junlian. Zhang had no choice but to lead the remaining soldiers out of the encirclement and retreated to Yingkou. When the Treaty of Shimonoseki was signed, Zhang retired to his hometown. Nie Shicheng was a subordinate of Ye Zhichao. In the Battle of Asan, Ye's army was defeated, and Nie was implicated. They retreated together, and Ye was punished. Nie then led a small force of a thousand men to defend Motian Ridge, protecting Shengjing. The Japanese army repeatedly attacked, but they were all driven away. Shengjing was preserved thanks to Nie's efforts.

The Same Wind and Snow, People in Two Different Places

— Yan Chonglou

A foreign-style building in Shanghai. The room is equipped with hot water radiators and an electric stove. The air is very warm. The owner is wearing a fox fur coat, embracing his beloved wife, drinking warm wine, and eating hot pot, while enjoying the snowflakes dancing outside the glass window. The owner is very interested in this cold and snowy weather.

A lonely camp outside the Great Wall. A biting cold wind blows into the camp from time to time. Water freezes into ice. The air is very bleak. The soldiers are wearing thin clothes, holding iron guns, enduring hunger, and shivering. They are vigilantly guarding against the enemy's ruthless bullets. The soldiers feel immense pain in this cold and snowy weather.

The same compatriots, why are the rich people sitting comfortably in Shanghai enjoying themselves, while the soldiers fighting the enemy outside the Great Wall are suffering so much? The same wind and snow, why does it bring joy to the eyes of the rich in Shanghai, but pain to the eyes of the soldiers resisting the enemy outside the Great Wall?

In the cold and snowy weather, I had the above doubts and feelings.

Also, during the Boxer Rebellion in the Gengzi year, the Eight-Nation Alliance arrived. On May 18, Dagu fell. Nie's vanguard was stationed at Zizhulin. The Japanese army arrived first, and Nie defeated them in one fell swoop, causing many deaths. The allied forces of other countries continued to advance. Nie fought hard, acting as one against a hundred. The allied forces knew that Nie was not easy to defeat, so they attacked him with green gas cannons. Nie died very tragically. Noble and outstanding generals, Zhang and Nie can be considered worthy of the title.

Mourning the Late Xu Zhimo

— Wu Tianfang

I returned to Shanghai from a mountain tour in Fenghua and saw in the newspaper that Zhimo had died tragically in a plane crash in Jinan. I was saddened all day. Gu Hongye, a literature professor at Jinan University, used to live in Liulimen, the old capital. One day, the host arranged a banquet. Among the guests were Zhimo and I. In the middle of the meal, Zhimo raised his glass to me and said, "Drink with the King of Balls as much as you can." Everyone present did not know who he was referring to. Alas, Zhimo was indeed my old friend. Sixteen or seventeen years ago, I was studying at Wulin Anding. Every time there was a soccer match, I always played center forward. At that time, Zhimo was a top student at Yizhong, coming to watch. Sometimes, he would participate in the game, rushing forward powerfully. This is how we became acquainted. The past is like dust. Now, we have not been friends for a long time, and I don't even remember talking about it. But Zhimo alone could mention it. Although I humbly declined, it cannot be said that he was not my old friend. For more than ten years, we have been busy with our own affairs and have not been in touch. Occasionally, we would meet on the road, wave to each other, and then pass by like wind and clouds. In the 17th year of the Republic, I traveled to Pengcheng and received a message from He Junjingwu, informing me of Zhimo's whereabouts. However, I never had the chance to meet him. I always remember his outstanding literary talent and unrestrained personality. When he was a classmate in the preparatory course at Peking University, he was already considered an outstanding figure. Later, he studied abroad, and his brilliance grew daily. Upon his return, he discussed literature with Mr. Ren Gong, Mr. Shizhi, Mr. Zong Meng, and others, and published new poems, creating a unique style. As a result, his reputation was great. His life can be described as truly being "small when placed among great figures, and not feeling great when squeezed among mediocre people," as Mr. Liu Haisu said. If Heaven had granted Zhimo another thirty-six years, his life would have been no more than seventy-two years. Would he have been hated by the world and said to have made no contribution to literature? How could he have died so young and so tragically? I attach a small collection of poems, cut in two, to express my mourning: "Golden hair and white hair fluttered in the wind, I did not see the orchid banner and cinnamon flag. Suddenly, an old friend passed through my heart, a crescent moon fell on the treetops in the long sky. The wind and rain in Wenyang made the six curtains black, the hundred walls of the city were filled with chaotic red. Heaven seemed to say, 'Your mother is in the north,' I heard the weeping south of the Yangtze River."

▲Mourning Zhimo, I have already expressed my grief with a poem and a couplet, but my feelings are not exhausted. I have composed another poem and attached it to a wreath to mourn him. Zhang Xiaoruo

China's poets are unmatched, one flight reports the loss of literature. The joys and sorrows of ice and frost all become dreams, the literary talent and grace are most extraordinary. The fierce tiger gathered together to pass on the unfinished work, creating a grave on the top of the mountain. In recent years, the feelings for the family and the country have been endless, and I cannot bear to hear the wild crying and the mourning of the wild geese.

▲The grief is still not exhausted, and I have composed two more quatrains to mourn the poet. Zhang Xiaoruo

In the cold of late winter, I look to Liaoyang, the moon is black and the sky is low, and the enemy is strong. The whole world is worried about the nest being overturned, how could he die in Zhengjiazhuang.

His fame spread throughout the sea, and his integrity was evident in his sincere friendship. Beyond the sky, the Ganges River and the clouds and trees are pure, and even more heartbreaking is the old poet.

Christmas Chicken

— Xiaoyan

According to Western customs, every year on New Year's Day and Christmas Day at the end of the year, every household prepares dishes, especially

Mr. Gao Junshan Talks About the National Crisis After Returning from Europe and America (3) Ji Ping

For example, as reported in the newspaper the day before yesterday, the chairman of the Special Committee's resignation contained the passage "... for several decades, world public opinion has been gathering sympathy for our country. International justice is gradually becoming clear. The third resolution of the League of Nations has been established. The diplomatic aspect has come to an end..." It seems that the countries are helping a lot in this Sino-Japanese incident, and our diplomacy is very victorious. It is natural to "come to an end" after losing the three northeastern provinces. If the whole country is lost, it will eventually "come to an end". If the government authorities are so optimistic, how can the people rest assured? Therefore, it is our misfortune, not our strength, that our people pay so much attention to politics.

In recent days, the newspapers have often reported that students have taken actions outside the norm. Generally, people regard this as a hidden worry. In fact, it is inevitable that some people will overstep the bounds due to patriotic movements. However, if one relies on the power of the masses to bully those who cannot resist, such as Wang Fusheng, then one will inevitably betray the original motive of the patriotic movement. Those who break the law should be dealt with according to the law. In today's civilized era, if there are behaviors such as torture as reported in the newspapers, it must be the idea of twenty-odd people. Pure patriotic youths would never take such action. I hope that students will recognize their goals and work towards them, and not be manipulated by a few corrupt elements, which would completely undo the efforts of the past few months.

Some people say that the League of Nations is a loot-sharing organization of the five major powers. It can be said that they are right. In principle, the League of Nations does not talk about "equality". This time, our country has suffered such great oppression and humiliation from Japan. We have no preparation and do not resist. We only dream of relying on the League of Nations to mediate. This is a fundamental mistake. We can understand the inequality and unreliability of the League of Nations itself with a very simple view.

(1) The League of Nations was born based on the Treaty of Versailles. This is a treaty of the victorious countries after the European War. In other words, it is a treaty that accommodates the powerful countries. Therefore, if a dispute occurs between a powerful country and a weak country, and a judgment is requested, the powerful country will definitely take advantage.

(2) According to the provisions of the Covenant, a resolution must be unanimously agreed upon before it can be passed. This method is specifically for the convenience of the powerful countries. Because of this provision, the powerful countries can go their own way without regard to public opinion. It is impossible to ask about their intentions when the Covenant was drafted. In this Sino-Japanese incident, Japan cast a dissenting vote, rendering the thirteen votes of the other countries ineffective. This is why we are suffering from this Covenant. If a weak country has any unique claims, it can only succumb to violence. There would be no hope of realization.

(3) The five permanent seats on the Council of the League of Nations are represented by the United Kingdom, France, Germany, Japan, and Italy. The remaining nine non-permanent seats are selected by the member states. It is clear that the League of Nations is controlled by the powerful.

Christmas Chicken

Christmas chicken, the Western name is turkey, commonly known as huoji (fire chicken), also known as qimianji (seven-faced chicken). Because the chicken's head is a mixture of red and blue, hideous and terrifying, it is also called Bailuji (White Dew Chicken). It is only gradually available on the market after the White Dew Festival. It is also called Tusouji (Spit Silk Chicken). The feathers of the chicken's body sometimes have a tail like a peacock's, like a brocade ribbon. Because its name is the same as "Turkey", it is also called Turkey Chicken. Recently, as Christmas Day and New Year's Day approach, this chicken has become a valuable commodity in Western industries. Dinghai in Zhejiang, that is, the Zhoushan Islands in the geographical record. In addition to fishing and farming, the islanders also raise this chicken. From hatching in the spring until the beginning of winter, the chicken has grown up. Male chickens are more valuable. The weight of a large one is always around 20 to 30 pounds. Transported to the sea, it is sold to Western restaurants. Each pound costs four or five dimes. The owner of the Family Restaurant at 296 Jing'an Temple Road, He Zhaoyu, is from Dinghai, so he transports fire chickens from his hometown to Shanghai himself. Those who like Western food must go to the Family Restaurant to eat fire chicken. This is also one of the common knowledge of eating in Shanghai. However, Europeans, except for New Year's Day and Christmas Day at the end of the year, do not have fire chicken unless they are entertaining distinguished guests. Only on Christmas Day, because every household must prepare this dish, it is also called Christmas Chicken.

The taste of fire chicken is slightly different from that of Chinese chicken. Chicken taste has no oily smell. Chicken meat is also more loose, dry, and delicious than Chinese chicken. The taste of roasted chicken is even better than that of roasted duck. When Europeans hire a chef, they always ask if they can roast fire chicken, which is regarded as a standard for employment. This also shows the importance Europeans attach to fire chicken.

Rotary Club Novel

Sharing the Same Hatred With You (17)

— Gu Mingdao

Chapter 4: Killing Relatives for Justice

Zhongshu lowered her head, seemingly deep in thought. The room was as quiet as if no one was there. Only the sounds of distant military bugles could be heard, wailing and sobbing, very desolate. After a long time, Zhongshu raised her head and said to Hua Naiqiang, "That's right. A person can only bravely choose one path to take, and cannot walk two paths at the same time. Weighing the pros and cons, I agree to follow your words." When Naiqiang heard her answer these few words, a look of surprise and joy appeared on his face. He bent over and bowed deeply to Zhongshu, very respectfully.

The next morning, the wind in T City picked up urgently. Peng Meiguo had ordered the troops in the capital to set off immediately to attack H Province. At the same time, a dozen or so officers from the Sun Country rushed to assist. It was said that dozens of cannons had been transported. The general populace was frightened. Although they did not approve of Peng Meiguo's treasonous actions, they could not do anything about him with their bare hands. Peng Meiguo, along with his chief of staff and several Sun Country officers, was about to set off when he suddenly caught sight of his daughter Zhongshu. She had already changed into a military uniform, wearing a military cap, and carrying a box cannon at her waist. She walked in from outside, looking like a young military officer, and said to Gu Meiguo, "Father is going to war, and I want to go with you. Let me gain some experience on the battlefield, and I can also protect Father." Peng Meiguo couldn't help but smile and said, "In ancient times there was Hua Mulan, and now there is Peng Zhongshu. It is truly a rare coincidence. Since you are willing to go, I will take you with me. Just don't be afraid of the sound of gunfire." Zhongshu said, "Father, don't underestimate your daughter. If I were afraid, I wouldn't have come to ask." The people around saw that the chief general's daughter was also joining the army, and they praised her as a female hero. Zhongshu saw that her father had agreed, and then said, "My classmate Hua Jun is here, and he also wants to set off together." Peng Meiguo nodded and said, "It's good for him to go for a walk." Then he saw a young man in military uniform walking in from outside, giving Peng Meiguo a military salute and standing aside. Peng Meiguo said, "Hua Jun, if you want to go with me, you must work hard with me. You must know that I am not relying on foreign forces to deceive my compatriots. It is really because China is in extreme internal turmoil. A group of young men are fighting for power and profit, regardless of national affairs. I have been in office for a long time, and although I have no great achievements, I sit idly by and watch those young men rise to prominence, making the people suffer even more. Therefore, I am sending troops this time to recover H Province and quell the internal turmoil, for the sake of saving the country and protecting the people. You should know this." Hua Naiqiang agreed with a "yes" word. In his heart, he was extremely angry, cursing the old thief. You are clearly harming the country and the people, and you still say you are saving the country and protecting the people. Where is your sense of shame? Peng Meiguo then ordered the two to follow him closely. He immediately took the train and set off, heading for H Province.

Securities Exchange Abolishes Bond Price Limits

▲ Agreed upon yesterday and will be implemented soon.

▲ Yesterday, many bonds had fallen to the price limit.

Yesterday, the market conditions of various bonds on the Chinese Merchants Securities Exchange showed that there were many types of spot transactions, and the inflow and outflow were not lonely. However, futures were becoming increasingly weak, and the transaction volume continued to be less than the previous day. For example, the salt tax fell to the lowest price limit in the morning, and the transaction volume became extremely scarce. Other bonds were also not as good as before. As for the price trend, the Sino-Japanese diplomatic situation continued to be quite serious, with plans to attack Jinzhou. The future was very dangerous, and the domestic situation showed little progress. The general sentiment in the market was weaker than before. In addition, the predetermined standard price limit restricted the market, preventing all parties from freely buying and selling. It was also feared that this would lead to further disputes in the future, because when the market price fell to the price limit, the exchange would no longer allow trading. On the brokerage side, those who had previously agreed to sell at the price limit for long-term customers were restricted and would not be able to close out. Therefore, if the prices continued to fall, the future would be a concern and would definitely affect future deliveries. The exchange observed this situation and reported the difficulties to the exchange supervisor, requesting the Ministry of Finance to abolish the price limit in order to stabilize the market. The exchange has now received a letter from the supervisor, allowing the exchange to discuss and find a proper solution. The exchange specially decided last night to abolish the previously set minimum price limit, so that the market can still trade freely without restrictions. This change may boost market sentiment, but yesterday, those who heard of the abolition of the price limit were very cautious. The buying transactions on the market were very cold. Although there was no large-scale selling, sporadic disposal was quite common, which made the market even more depressed. The market price of various bonds continued to fall, and the trend did not weaken slightly. Among them, the salt tax reached the minimum price limit at the beginning of the morning market. Other bonds also fell sharply, but since the initial session, although the prices were still falling, the trend was always very peaceful. As a result, except for the salt tax, which had already fallen close to the price limit the day before, and the 96 customs tax, which also fell by only a few jiao, all others fell by 1 yuan to 1.89 yuan. In addition, spot goods such as post-war military supplies and disaster relief, which had not been traded for many months, suddenly started trading yesterday, and the price drop was also very large. The total spot transactions yesterday were 22,200 yuan, futures were 3.6 million in the morning and over 2.3 million in the afternoon, totaling 5.945 million yuan.

Yesterday, U.S. cotton initially weakened due to pressure from sellers, but then firmed due to strong support from Wall Street and short covering. U.S. Cotton Market Relatively Stable Last Week

A telegram from New York on the 18th reports on the cotton market for the week: The cotton market was particularly calm last week, with limited price fluctuations. Although the overall trend showed no improvement, sentiment was more resilient. Although stock market fluctuations exerted pressure on raw cotton, they proved ineffective. Later, the South made some hedging sales, but the supply there remained thin. Furthermore, short covering and buying by industry players helped maintain prices. Japan's strict ban on gold exports and the devaluation of the Japanese yen seemed likely to restrict Japan's spot purchases from the South. However, as far as the long-staple cotton they had previously imported was concerned, it seemed sufficient to meet their needs for the entire season. Moreover, they will be suspending the gold standard, which further demonstrates the good position of their textile industry, enabling it to compete with Lancashire in the world.

Grains: Rice from Hexia Affected by Rain

▲ Nantou: Yesterday, the source of supplies for various groups was still not abundant, with approximately ten or so ships arriving. The inventory in Pu Cun was thick. The price of thick new japonica rice increased by about 0.10 yuan. Although there were not many high-quality foreign Du rice, the sales were average. The overall trend was fixed, and fluctuations were insignificant.

▲ Xinzha: The source of supplies coming down from Suzhou Creek was not abundant, and there was a slight accumulation in the river. Due to the rainy weather, transactions in this street were scarce. However, the trading houses that were open were only Tongxing, Heyu, Changxiang, and Hengxing, with approximately 2,000 dan. The goods that will be sold tomorrow include two types: Changxi, Xixin, and Nanhang thin rice. The quotations are 0.10 yuan each. The other goods have not yet been traded. Due to the light rain, the goods on the ships have not yet been opened.

Foreign Rice Sales Suspended Again

Yesterday in the foreign rice market, the purchases by various customer groups were suspended again. However, there were still dealings within the street, so the market was able to stabilize. The Tongshi opened with 300 bags of No. 1 Saigon at a price of 10.08 yuan, and 500 bags of small broken rice at a price of 9.17 yuan. The futures market was also fixed. Foreign firms were also selling. Yesterday, Xiangmao sold 2,000 tons of February small broken rice at a price of 4.27 taels, and Taihe sold 2,000 tons of May small broken rice at a price of 4.6 taels, which were bought by firms in Zhabei and other places. New Taizhou white rice arrived yesterday and 1,000 bags were also traded in this city at a price of 9.65 yuan to 9.23 yuan. The street scene was also stable.

Near and Far Term Flour Show Good Signs

Yesterday, after the opening of the flour market in the morning and afternoon, the market conditions for each month generally turned to a stable and brisk trend. The quotations for foreign wheat rebounded by about 0.04 to 0.06 yuan. In addition, the gold market was not affected by the suspension of exchange and had stabilized. The near-term flour was also quite active due to some purchases by the Nanyang gang. Therefore, both near and far term flour showed good signs. However, because flour factories had ordered two more ships of foreign wheat, they continued to sell off. Under these circumstances, there was little hope for a price increase in the future. As a result, this month was 0.01 yuan better than the previous day, January and February were 0.015 yuan better, March was 0.01 yuan better, April was 0.005 yuan better, and May was 0.0025 yuan better.

Wheat Futures Mixed

Yesterday, after the opening of the wheat futures market in the morning and afternoon, the market conditions for each month generally showed a fluctuating trend. Because today was the last day of the month, the factory's purchases were only twenty or thirty trucks, but there was quite a lot of wheat on the market, so the trend was flat. As for the distant months, since foreign wheat quotations had risen, they should have increased. However, it was rumored that the factories had ordered foreign wheat, one ship of Canadian red wheat with January loading for only 3.63 taels, and one ship of Australian western wheat with April loading for only 3.73 taels. Therefore, sentiment was very flat, and the distant term saw a slight decrease. As a result, this month was down 0.03 yuan from the previous day, January was unchanged, February was up 0.01 yuan, March was down 0.01 yuan, and April and May were down 0.02 yuan.

Sugar Market: Taikoo Sugar Declines and Rises

▲ Taikoo Sugar Declines and Rises

Yesterday, the sugar market production area telegrams stated that the price of Cuban raw sugar was 1.09375, a decrease of 0.03125 from the previous telegram. The price of New York sugar futures for December was 1.01, for March next year 1.05, for May 1.2, and for September 1.12, a decrease of 0.03 to 0.05 from the previous prices. The prices of current and forward Java sugar still lacked ups and downs. The association market was planning to increase prices, and the market atmosphere turned strong, with trading quite active. Dutch sugar No. 24 coarse granulated white sugar for export was raised, and ice sugar factories made slight returns, with a transaction price of 9.475 taels. The market conditions were very brisk. Fine ground granulated white sugar was 9.525 to 9.55 taels, and No. 20 medium granulated white sugar was 9.4 taels, with a firm trend. Taikoo Sugar B mark was 11.65 to 11.75 taels, HX mark was 11.45 to 11.5 taels, and CW mark was 11.55 taels. Trading was still prosperous, and the future prices were all called higher. The Hua Xin Hao sold over 500 bags of CW mark at a price of 11.55 taels. The trade intention was quite strong, and the sale was completed in an instant. The market conditions were all brisk. Looking at the sugar market trend, it seemed that there was still room for a gradual increase.

Silk, Tea and Foreign Firms: Silk Sales Almost Stagnant

Yesterday, the foreign firm silk market in this port almost stagnated. The exchange rate fluctuated, overseas silk reports did not transfer, and general hoarding households, in view of the depression of the European and American silk markets, did not dare to hoard. The market atmosphere was silent. Yesterday, only Samsung purchased 5 bales of small car yellow factory silk, and Mei Da purchased 5 bales of yellow silk, with prices still flat.

New York Guangdong Silk Falls with Japanese Silk

▲　　　　　　Style　　　　　　　Gold One Jiao

New York Raw Silk Market, the price of silk from China, Japan, Italy and France has fallen across the board due to the sharp fall in Yokohama Japanese silk. The price of Guangdong new-style white factory silk has always followed the Japanese silk. According to a New York telegram yesterday, the current market price of Guangdong new-style high-quality white factory silk is only 1.8 U.S. dollars per pound, a drop of 0.10 U.S. dollars compared to last week.

Waterproof American Raincoat Fabric Continues to Decline

Single-sided waterproof American raincoat fabric is the most widely sold, and both Chinese and Western clothing require it. All customer groups purchase it, and all flannel shops sell it. The sales volume increases every year. Recently, the waterproof American raincoat fabric has been falling daily. Since the British exchange rate increased, it has continued to decline. Goods that previously sold for over 5 taels are now reduced to 4.5 taels, and it is still possible to select colors and split bolts after deducting commissions. The main reason is that the increase in the British exchange rate has greatly increased orders, and the cost of goods is lower. It is heard that a large amount will continue to arrive next month.

Coal: White Coal Dust Sells at High Prices

Recently, various white coal dusts have been greatly absorbed by various coal briquette factories in this port due to increased uses, resulting in very little circulation of spot goods on the market, and the plate price has therefore risen sharply. Yesterday, the market price of Shanxi coal was 10 taels per ton, an increase of about 0.75 taels compared to last week's selling price. Furthermore, Hongqi coal dust is the most scarce in stock and is quite difficult to purchase. The selling price per ton has also risen by 0.05 taels, and the current selling price is 11.25 taels per ton.

Local News

National Crisis Relief Association of the Republic of China Established Yesterday

Since the establishment of the Jiangsu National Crisis Relief Association, people from various provinces in Shanghai have responded enthusiastically. After several discussions, the inaugural meeting of the National Crisis Relief Association of the Republic of China was held yesterday. More than 500 people from 16 provinces attended. Chu Fucheng, Wen Zongyao, Peng Yunyi, and Zhang Yaozeng were elected as the presidium. The meeting passed the association's charter, declaration, and telegram, and resolved to oppose military rule. Finally, directors and supervisors were elected and the meeting adjourned. The declaration is recorded below: "Declaration of the National Crisis Relief Association of the Republic of China" The saying goes, "People must insult themselves before others insult them; a country must attack itself before others attack it." After the European War, even the weak and small nations of the world, under the aegis of justice and humanity, have established nations and striven for self-determination. Yet our ancient and great Chinese nation, in broad daylight, is being wantonly trampled upon in its sovereignty and its land seized, staging an unprecedented humiliation since the founding of the Republic. Who is responsible for this, and why has it come to this? The brutal and unbridled Japanese militarists are certainly intolerable to the world's justice, but the blame for our nation's self-inflicted insults in recent years cannot be excused either. What is meant by self-insult? Looking at it comprehensively from political and social perspectives, the details are too numerous to mention. Only the greatest and most obvious will be discussed. A group of people within the country advocates party rule, seizes political power, and positions itself as the ruling class, disregarding the status of the majority of citizens as masters of the nation. This is the first self-insult. This group has never lacked clear doctrines, political programs, and policies, but when exercising governing power, they often contradict themselves. The military administration does not focus on national defense planning, but only on internal strife. The financial administration does not focus on production and construction, but only on extravagance. The diplomatic administration does not focus on sound and effective strategies and unwavering preparation, but only on empty rhetoric. All measures are designed to embellish peace and prosperity to deceive the people. This is the second self-insult. Having formed a party, factions within the party are divided and stand opposed to each other, forgetting the important mission of nation-building entrusted to them, and only knowing how to exploit their special status to compete for public and private power. This is the third self-insult. People outside the party have reverted to the pre-Republic era of not discussing politics. Regarding major national policies, they either remain silent or resort to murmuring in private, never stepping forward with a bright, upright, and responsible attitude to help the country. This is the fourth self-insult. When things rot, worms breed. With the nation insulting and attacking itself in this way, how can we expect a powerful enemy not to insult and attack us? Now that a great disaster has erupted, and a great mistake has been made, has our nation awakened? Has it repented? Then, starting from today, let us sweep away the roots of self-insult and self-attack between parties, between parties and the people, and between the people themselves. Let us forge the 400 million people into one, to stand together as masters of the nation, to jointly shoulder the mission of rescuing the weak and extinguishing the flames. Those who looked down upon and insulted each other in the past should transform into mutual love and mutual assistance, truly united and truly striving, learning from the French people after the Franco-Prussian War, learning from the German people after the European War. With the goal of restoring the integrity of the territory of the Republic of China and ending the national crisis, even if the enemy's offensive is fierce, it will surely restrain itself one day. Even if the national situation is precarious, it will surely strengthen itself one day. The key lies in whether our people can unite and realize the principle of sovereignty residing in the people. The situation is urgent. We, the members, respectfully respond to the psychology of our people who refuse to insult themselves, initiate this association as an expression of national unity, to open up a path to remedy and save the country. Fellow countrymen, come and join us!

Song Qingling's Declaration

Song Qingling yesterday issued a personal declaration, saying, "The Kuomintang has long lost its status as a revolutionary group. This has become an undeniable fact today. What destroys the Kuomintang is not its external enemies, but its internal leaders. Since Mr. Sun's death in Beiping in the fourteenth year, the National Revolution suddenly lost its mentor, almost leading to its interruption. Fortunately, the comrades in Guangdong at that time恪遵Mr. Sun's teachings, took the masses as the foundation of the revolution. The Northern Expeditionary Force was eventually able to pacify the Yangtze River Basin in the shortest possible time. However, since the separation of Ning and Han in the sixteenth year, due to Chiang Kai-shek's personal dictatorship and the contention between warlords and bureaucrats, the party and the masses have increasingly drifted apart, using anti-communism as a pretext to carry out reactionary actions, using all kinds of阴很险毒, corruption, and deception. At the central level, they occupy important positions, operating for personal gain and consolidating their positions. At the local level, they oppress the people, acting tyrannically. Opportunistic remnants of warlords can leap to become the mainstay of the party-state, while loyal revolutionary talents must be found a way to put to death. The recent tragic killing of Deng Yanda, who was坚苦卓絶, loyal, brave, and奋发, is one example. In the past five years, internal wars and political struggles have continued endlessly. The party has disintegrated, and they have not hesitated to beg for pity from imperialism, using corrupt forces to do everything that the Beiyang warlords and bureaucrats dared not do, all of which is brazenly done in the name of party rule, making the party bear the unjust charge, incurring the hatred and contempt of the people across the country. In fact, the Three Principles of the People have never been put into practice for a single day. Recently, the confrontation between Ning and Guangdong has exposed each other's shortcomings, boasting of their strengths. 'Political openness,' 'democratic centralism,' 'revolutionary diplomacy,' all kinds of terms are not unpleasant to hear, but in reality, both rely on warlords, flatter imperialism, betray the masses, and are both criminals of the revolution. Since the outbreak of the Japanese invasion of Manchuria, both sides, forced by the national crisis and public opinion, have had to temporarily suspend their internecine warfare, carrying out their so-called peaceful unification, running around for meetings, which has lasted for more than three months. The focus of the debate is the distribution of central committee members and the selection of high-ranking officials, without a word of discussion on the suffering and interests of the vast majority of peasants and workers. They do not know that the creation of dictatorship, the degeneration of the party, and the decline of the country are all the results of being separated from the peasants and workers. Only by taking peasants and workers as the mainstay of the revolution can the degeneration of revolutionary forces be prevented and the foundation of the national economy be established. Apart from this, speaking of peaceful unification, even if it proceeds smoothly and everyone gets what they want, the result will only be peaceful division of spoils and unified evildoing. What joy do the people have in seeing this peace? What value does the country have in having this unification? I cannot bear to see the revolutionary foundation painstakingly built by Mr. Sun for forty years destroyed by a small number of selfish and self-interested ambitious party members, and I especially do not want to see the country of 400 million Chinese people destroyed by the Chinese Kuomintang, which betrays its own principles. I must at this time offer my most straightforward and sincere advice. Mr. Sun established the party for the revolution. If the party cannot save the country and benefit the people, what is there to be concerned about in self-destruction? I firmly believe that only a revolutionary force that is truly based on the masses and fights for the masses can eliminate warlords and bureaucrats, eradicate imperialism, and realize socialism. At the same time, I deeply believe that China's true revolutionaries will not be passively afraid and shrink back because of the terror and killing of reactionary forces, but will instead strengthen their determination to sacrifice and fight due to the pressure of the environment and the cries of the masses, regardless of everything, and advance together on the great road of revolution. December 19, 20th year, Song Qingling."

▲Conference Staff: Presidium: Fu Dewei, Zhou Xuexiang, Zhu Xuefan, Li Yongxiang, Yu Xianting; Recorders: Miao Hongjun, Zhao Shusheng

▲Matters Resolved: (1) Proposal to establish the Shanghai Special Municipality General Labor Union; (2) Proposal to abolish the current Trade Union Law and Labor Regulations, and to request the authorities to promulgate a Trade Union Law and Labor Regulations that effectively protect workers' organizations based on the Trade Union Organization Regulations of the 13th year of the Republic of China, and to have worker representatives attend and participate in the drafting; (3) Proposal that the authorities shall not distinguish or discriminate workers based on their knowledge, profession, or service organization, and should uniformly maintain their special rights to organize trade unions; (4) Proposal that the government should effectively implement relief for unemployed workers; (5) Proposal to support the Fourth Plenary Session of the First Central Committee and improve party and government organizations; (6) Proposal to suggest that the authorities determine a revolutionary policy towards Japan and vigorously implement revolutionary diplomacy to restore national rights and territory; (7) Proposal to unite the people of the whole country to persist in the thorough economic severance with Japan; (8) Proposal to re-telegram workers in various countries around the world, declaring the atrocities of the violent Japan and various acts that undermine world peace, in order to arouse the sympathy and assistance of various countries; (9) Proposal to issue a solemn declaration by the Representative Assembly; (10) Proposal to telegraph the Fourth Plenary Session of the First Central Committee in the name of the Assembly, ordering the military commanders in charge to recover the lost territories; (11) Proposal that after the establishment of the City General Labor Union, the National Labor Unions should be convened as soon as possible to establish the National General Labor Union to protect the interests of workers and concentrate forces to confront foreign aggression; (12) Proposal to issue a declaration in the name of the Assembly to support the striking workers of the Datong Bookstore and Dahua Match Factory; (13) Proposal to issue a declaration and announcement in the name of various labor unions attending the Assembly to support the Special Municipality General Labor Union; (14) Proposal that members of the General Labor Union shall not receive salaries. All of the above proposals were unanimously passed. At the end, the entire body of representatives shouted slogans and went to the Liguang Photography Studio to take a photo before dispersing.

▲Executive and Supervisory Personnel Elected: Fu Dewei, Li Yong, Zhu Xuefan, Zhao Zhenhui, Li Mengnan, Chen Haiqiu, Yu Xianting, Long Peiyun, Weng Ruifu, Gong Yuting, Zhou Xuexiang, Ge Hecai, Sang Yutang, Mei Guozhen, Zhang Linhua, Zhao Shusheng, Shao Xubai, Liu Xingbo, Chen Qingrong, and 19 others were elected as executive committee members. Hu Peiji, Sun Liang, Zhang Yiping, and three others were elected as alternate supervisory committee members.

▲Solemn Declaration: The Shanghai Labor Union Representative Assembly solemnly declares regarding the establishment of the Shanghai Special Municipality General Labor Union, "Our Party takes leading the masses and striving for revolution as its banner. The past revolutionary achievements were all due to the majority of the masses fighting and striving under the leadership of our Party, so the Party's strength could be concentrated and the Party's foundation could be consolidated. However, since the sixteenth year of the Republic of China, the leaders of the Party have often been reluctant to shoulder the responsibility of leadership, and a small number of corrupt and degenerate elements have taken the opportunity to infiltrate the Party. The fact that the Party itself has become alienated from, deceived, and oppressed the masses has become increasingly apparent. The masses, in their disappointment, have criticized the Party and lost their faith. As a result, domestic politics has also lost its important center, leading to the current crisis of fragmentation and disintegration. Today, the people of the whole country are looking forward to the revival of the Party's rule. It is imperative to plan without delay. We, the members, dare to jointly issue the following propositions from the standpoint of the people: A. Regarding Party affairs: 1. The Party takes democratic centralism as its principle. Future organizations and facilities should be absolutely democratized, and under no circumstances should the mistakes of past dictatorship be repeated under any name. 2. The Party takes the masses as its foundation and should effectively integrate with the masses to enrich itself and fulfill its responsibility to lead the masses in carrying out its principles. 3. The Party is the greatest driving force in national politics, and all political and military affairs should be subject to the Party's control, so as to implement the principle of governing the country through the Party. 4. Party and government personnel in charge should not hold concurrent positions, so as to avoid the evils of the Party hindering the government or the government encroaching on the Party. B. Regarding the mass movement: The mass movement should be guided by the Party, but its independence and freedom must be respected. C. Regarding the labor movement: 1. Raise the status of workers and protect workers' organizations. 2. Abolish the current Trade Union Law and all labor laws and regulations, and re-enact Trade Union Law and Labor Regulations that effectively protect workers' organizations based on the labor laws and regulations personally drafted by Premier Sun in the thirteenth year, and formally appoint representatives from the labor circle to attend and participate in the drafting of the regulations. 3. Workers' organizations have vertical and horizontal organizations, and their establishment is supported. 4. Workers shall not be distinguished or discriminated against based on their knowledge, profession, or service organization, and shall have the right to organize trade unions equally. 5. The government authorities should provide effective relief to unemployed workers. 6. Recognize the workers' absolute right to strike freely. 7. Restore the original organizations of various workers' and trade unions during the eighteenth year of the Republic of China. 8. Support the organization of trade unions by unorganized workers. The above points are the most salient. Detailed plans still need to be confirmed and implemented one by one by the Party and state officials and gentlemen from all walks of life. As for the propositions on diplomacy and the Sino-Japanese issue, they have been seen in previous telegrams and declarations, and will not be repeated here. We, the members, will not forget the legacy and have unanimously resolved to establish the Shanghai City General Labor Union today in order to rectify the workers' movement and implement labor policies, unite the strength of workers throughout the city, and continue to fight, so that the city's labor movement can enter the right track and the Party and state's future can gradually move towards a bright future. This is not only the goal of our 800,000 fellow workers working with sincerity and effort, but also the great plan that 400 million compatriots earnestly pray for. From now on, our 800,000 fellow workers throughout the city will be dear, sincere, and united, upholding principles under the leadership of the Party and the City General Labor Union, acting according to the right path, striving to revitalize industries, and improve labor welfare. We hope that the Party and state officials and domestic sages will not hesitate to impart their wisdom and provide assistance from time to time, so that not only will our fellow workers throughout the city be eternally grateful, but the future of the Party and the state will truly rely on it. Shanghai City Labor Representatives Assembly."

▲Establishment Telegram: The Shanghai Special Municipality General Labor Union's establishment telegram states, "To all levels of Party headquarters, provincial, municipal, and county governments, all groups, all newspapers, and all compatriots across the country: On the 19th of this month, the Shanghai City Labor Representatives Assembly was held and resolved to establish the 'Shanghai Special Municipality General Labor Union,' and elected Fu Dewei, Li Yongxiang, Zhu Xuefan, Zhao Zhenhui, Li Mengnan, Chen Haiqiu, Yu Xianting, Long Peiyun, Weng Ruifu, Gong Yuting, Zhou Xuexiang, Ge Hecai, Sang Yutang, Mei Guozhen, Zhang Linhua, Zhao Shusheng, Shao Xubai, Liu Xingbo, Chen Qingrong, and 19 others as executive committee members, and Ye Qiming, Zhang Zhurong, Wang Yuxiang, Xie Yutong, Wan Pusheng, Ye Xianggao, Miao Hongjun, Wang Jianping, Le Yaqing, and nine others as supervisory committee members, and Shi Ziqing, Liu Zupei, Li Junfeng, Wang Bingquan, Chen Deheng, Wu Bochao, Fan Yifeng, Chen Deyong, Liu Jintai, and nine others as alternate executive committee members, and Hu Peiji, Sun Liang, Zhang Yiping, and three others as alternate supervisory committee members. In addition to submitting this to the Fourth Plenary Session of the First Central Committee for filing and sending separate letters to the municipal Party and government and various institutions for their information, the office will be temporarily located at No. 9 Runde Lane, Fusheng Road, Zhabei, starting from today, and will begin operations. We hope that all sectors will not hesitate to impart their wisdom and provide assistance from time to time, for which we are immensely grateful. Shanghai Special Municipality General Labor Union, December 19th."

What Was Heard After the Disputes at the Municipal Chamber of Commerce

▲ The Municipal Chamber of Commerce Conducted Business as Usual Yesterday

▲ The Commercial Movement Committee Held a Representative Assembly Yesterday

▲ News from the Municipal Chamber of Commerce

After the Shanghai Special Municipality Commercial Movement Committee sent Zhao Nangong, Liu Musu, Chen Zhiying, and three others to take over the Shanghai Municipal Chamber of Commerce the day before yesterday without success, the Municipal Government ordered the Public Security Bureau and the Municipal Defense Corps to send police to protect all departments of the chamber, which continued to operate as usual. Yesterday, the chamber also convened a joint meeting of all executive and supervisory committee members, resolving to issue a joint statement and send two urgent telegrams expressing support for Mr. Wang Jingwei's national salvation conference and requesting Chen

Page 18

Mingshu, Wu Tiecheng, and Shao Lizi to come to Shanghai as soon as possible to guide Shanghai's party affairs. The following are recordings of various news reports:

▲ Held a Joint Meeting of Executive and Supervisory Committee Members Yesterday afternoon at 2:00 PM, the Municipal Chamber of Commerce held an emergency joint meeting of all executive committee members and supervisory committee members. Those present included Ye Huijun, Wang Xiaolai, Wang Yansong, Yuan Ludeng, Lu Wenshao, Lu Fengzhu, Wu Zhihao, Xu Jiqing, Lu Qinghua, Fang Jiaobo, Cai Yunqing, Zhu Wenqi, Wen Lanting, Cheng Xiechun, Lao Jingxiu, Lu Qisheng, Chen Songyuan, Feng Jiliang, Xiang Songmao, Jiang Zhigang, and others, totaling twenty people. Wang Xiaolai presided over the meeting. After the formalities, the chairman reported in detail on the disturbances that occurred the day before yesterday and read out the letter from the Shanghai Special Municipality Commercial Movement Committee. Subsequently, the committee members expressed their opinions, all expressing great indignation. After three hours of discussion, it was resolved: (1) To express satisfaction with the measures taken by the standing committee to deal with the temporary emergency situation and to ratify all its actions; (2) To pass the chamber's urgent declaration; (3) To issue a joint statement in the name of all executive and supervisory committee members, expressing a firm stance.

▲ Issued a Joint Statement The entire executive and supervisory committee of the Shanghai Municipal Chamber of Commerce issued a joint statement yesterday stating that the entire executive and supervisory committee of the Shanghai Municipal Chamber of Commerce believes that the so-called Shanghai Special Municipality Commercial Movement Committee's disturbance of the chamber on the 18th of this month, leading a crowd of plainclothes individuals, constitutes a complete act of destruction. Therefore, after convening a joint meeting of the executive and supervisory committees on the 19th of this month, it was resolved to issue the following joint statement: (1) The Shanghai Municipal Chamber of Commerce was formally established on June 22nd of the 19th year of the Republic of China, in accordance with the Chamber of Commerce Law promulgated by the National Government on August 15th of the 18th year of the Republic of China. At that time, the members of various industry associations who attended numbered 129, and the store members numbered 23, totaling 297 member representatives. Furthermore, Central Party Headquarters representative Yu Wenxian, National Government and Municipal Government representative Pan Gongzhan, Ministry of Industry and Commerce representative Zhao Jinqing, and National Commercial Federation Chairman Lin Kanghou all attended and provided guidance. Huijun, Lanting, and others were elected as executive committee members and supervisory committee members by the attending members through legal voting at the general meeting on that day. This is the process by which the chamber was legally established and the committee members were legally elected. (2) The Chamber of Commerce Law was passed by the Legislative Yuan on July 20th of the 18th year of the Republic of China, during Mr. Hu Hanmin's tenure as the head of the Legislative Yuan, and was promulgated by the National Government. In accordance with this law, there are clear and detailed regulations regarding the terms of office and re-election procedures for executive and supervisory committee members. Even if an officer is dismissed or ordered to resign due to cause, there must be sufficient reason and legal procedures. Therefore, the members of this chamber, in accordance with national laws and the public opinion entrusted by the members, cannot accept anyone using any name or illegal means or coercion to demand a handover. (3) According to the letter from the Shanghai Special Municipality Commercial Movement Committee to this chamber, delivered by Zhao Nangong, it stated, "It has been found that the Shanghai Special Municipality General Chamber of Commerce was illegally reorganized by the Nanjing Central Party Headquarters in April of the 18th year of the Republic of China." This is even more suspicious. When was the Shanghai Special Municipality Commercial Movement Committee established? According to the announcement of the committee published in the announcement column of various newspapers on the 18th of this month, it states that it was organized "by order." However, it has not clearly stated what kind of order it was issued under. Upon investigation, at the time of unifying the Shanghai merchant organization in the 18th year of the Republic of China, the central executive committee members were Jiang Zhongzheng, Dai Chuanxian, He Yingqin, Hu Hanmin, Xi Ke, Yan Xishan, Chen Guofu, Chen Mingshu, Zhu Peide, Ye Chucang, Wu Tiecheng, Feng Yuxiang, Yu Youren, Song Qingling, Song Ziwen, Wang Zhaoming, Wu Chaochu, He Chengjun, Li Wenfan, Wang Boling, Shao Yuanchong, Zhu Jiahua, Zhang Qun, Liu Zhi, Yang Shuzhuang, Fang Zhenwu, Zhao Daiwen, Zhou Qigang, Chen Lifu, Chen Zhaoying, Liu Jiwen, Liu Luyin, Ding Weifen, Zeng Yangfu, Fang Juehui, and 35 others. The central supervisory committee members were Wu Jingheng, Zhang Renjie, Gu Yingfen, Lin Sen, Cai Yuanpei, Zhang Ji, Wang Chonghui, Shao Lizi, Li Shizeng, Deng Zeru, Xiao Focheng, Enke Batu, and 12 others. At that time, the country was unified, and the party headquarters had not split. Not only had the current Extraordinary Conference of the Central Committee in Guangzhou not yet been established, but even the previous Enlarged Conference had not yet been produced. The figures in charge of the current Extraordinary Conference of the Central Committee in Guangzhou, such as Xiao Focheng, Deng Zeru, Gu Yingfen, Sun Ke, Wang Zhaoming, Wu Chaochu, Li Wenfan, Liu Jiwen, and other gentlemen, were all members of the Central Executive and Supervisory Committees at that time. The case of unifying the Shanghai Special Municipality merchant organization was resolved by the 7th Standing Committee Meeting of the Central Committee on May 2nd of the 18th year. The chairman of that meeting was Committee Member Sun Ke. The resolutions were: (1) All Shanghai Special Municipality merchant organizations shall cease activities. (2) Yu Qiaqing and 34 others shall be appointed as members of the reorganization committee. Furthermore, on May 16th, the 13th Standing Committee Meeting of the Central Committee resolved that the Shanghai Merchant Organization Reorganization Committee shall act on behalf of the former Shanghai Businessmen's Association, the Shanghai General Chamber of Commerce, the Zhabei Chamber of Commerce, and the Nanshi Chamber of Commerce, and appointed Hu Hanmin and six other committee members to draft the organizational outline of the reorganization committee. The chairman of that meeting was Committee Member Ye Chucang. Furthermore, on May 23rd, the 14th Standing Committee Meeting of the Central Committee passed the organizational outline of the reorganization committee. The chairman of that meeting was Committee Member Hu Hanmin. Now, the Shanghai Special Municipality Commercial Movement Committee accuses the Nanjing Central Party Headquarters of illegal reorganization, which means that they consider the resolutions of the three Central Party Affairs meetings chaired by Committee Members Sun Ke, Ye Chucang, and Hu Hanmin to be illegal. The committee members of this chamber do not know how it can be considered legal. (4) Since the National Government promulgated the Chamber of Commerce Law, it has repeatedly issued clear orders to reorganize according to the law within a prescribed time limit. In the north, the General Chambers of Commerce of Peiping and Tianjin were reorganized into the Peiping Municipal Chamber of Commerce and the Tianjin Municipal Chamber of Commerce. In the south, the Guangzhou General Chamber of Commerce was also reorganized into the Guangzhou Municipal Chamber of Commerce. The formal establishment of this municipal chamber of commerce was extremely proper and legal. Now, the Commercial Movement Committee believes that it is necessary to restore the Shanghai Special Municipality General Chamber of Commerce, and it is not known on what legal basis it is based. (5) The actions of a group should be bound by the will of the members of the group's organization. The various guilds, public offices, and public associations affiliated with the former Shanghai Special Municipality General Chamber of Commerce have now been reorganized into various industry associations according to the law. Today's newspapers have published a joint statement by 160 industry associations opposing this illegal action. The public opinion is already clearly visible. As for the officers of the former Shanghai Special Municipality General Chamber of Commerce: (1) There were a total of three chairmen: Mr. Feng Shaoshan, Mr. Lin Kanghou, and Mr. Zhao Jinqing. When the Municipal Chamber of Commerce was established, Mr. Zhao Jinqing was serving as the director of the Shanghai office of the Ministry of Industry and Commerce and came to give instructions on behalf of the Ministry of Industry and Commerce. Mr. Lin Kanghou also attended the meeting and delivered a speech as the chairman of the National Federation of Chambers of Commerce. (2) There were a total of four standing committee members: Mr. Lu Fengzhu, Mr. Ying Zhikun, Mr. Hu Xisheng, and Mr. Xu Jiqing. Mr. Lu Fengzhu, Mr. Hu Xisheng, and Mr. Xu Jiqing all served as members of the Commercial Reorganization Committee. Mr. Hu Xisheng also served as the director of the finance department of the Commercial Reorganization Committee. Currently, Mr. Xu Jiqing is a standing committee member of this chamber, and Mr. Lu Fengzhu is an executive committee member of this chamber. (3) There were 52 executive committee members. Among them, except for Mr. Huang Chujiu, Mr. Chen Caibao, Mr. Xu Qingyun, and Mr. Tao Meisheng, who have passed away, among the remaining 48, Sun Jingxi, Pei Yunqing, Wang Jiean, Fu Zuoheng, Wu Weiru, Yu Qiaqing, Wen Lanting, Xu Busun, Chen Canglai, Ye Huijun, Chen Yushu, Ye Fuxiao, Yuan Ludeng, Zhu Wenqi, Lao Jingxiu, Wu Zhihao, Xu Tingzuo, Yao Dexin, Zheng Xitang, Lu Peiyuan, Gu Xin, Chen Liangyu, Yan Junan, Chen Yizhou, You Senting, Chen Songyuan, and 26 others are now member representatives of this chamber. Furthermore, eight of them are current executive and supervisory committee members of this chamber. If the Commercial Reorganization Committee was illegally reorganized, and the Municipal Chamber of Commerce was also illegally established, and it is necessary to restore the former Shanghai Special Municipality General Chamber of Commerce, then why did most of the officers of the former General Chamber of Commerce either come to this chamber to give speeches or serve as members of this chamber, and not consider it illegal? Moreover, among the 22 current executive and supervisory committee members of this chamber, ten are former committee members of the General Chamber of Commerce. Now, Mr. Wang Jingwei is advocating the construction of democratic politics, with the sovereignty of the country residing in the people, and politics must seek democracy. The main body of the Chamber of Commerce is the industry association, and it must also take the will of the industry association as its will. If a small minority acts to violently seize the Chamber of Commerce, and its establishment goes against the public opinion of businessmen and the destruction of the spirit of the rule of law, then it is even more deeply believed by the members of this chamber. The above five points are a joint statement based on legal principles and facts, calmly and quietly, hoping that the government authorities, party and state leaders, and people from all walks of life, the entire business community, will give it practical consideration and make a fair judgment. The members of this chamber will never abandon their responsibilities unless through legally prescribed procedures. They will not yield to force and will only act in accordance with the law. We respectfully inform the people of the country. The first executive committee members of the Shanghai Municipal Chamber of Commerce are Huijun, Wang Xiaolai, Wang Yansong, Yuan Ludeng, Lu Wenshao, Lu Fengzhu, Wu Zhihao, Xu Ji, Luo Qinghua (Fang Jiaobo, Pei Huoqing, Zhu Wenqi, Ju Songsun, Gu Xin Yi, Xiang Songmao. The first supervisory committee members are Wen Lanting, Cheng Fenchun, Lao Jingxiu, Lu Qisheng, Chen Songyuan Ma Jiliang, Jiang Zhigang, December 19th, 20th year of the Republic of China

▲ Qin Runqing Issued a Statement Mr. Qin Runqing, chairman of the industry association, issued a statement yesterday saying that he regrets the disputes that occurred at the Municipal Chamber of Commerce yesterday. At a time when foreign troubles are pressing and internal worries are mounting, it is appropriate to unite as one to seek external solutions. Moreover, with the end of the year approaching, financial relations are particularly important. If disputes are re-ignited, affecting the market, the impact will be great. He sincerely hopes that all parties will understand and not repeat the suffering of our people.

▲ Three Associations Deny Being Listed The cotton cloth, refined products, and department store industry associations issued a statement denying that they were listed in the notice of the meeting convened by the Commercial Movement Committee, stating that today, our associations received a notice, which was headed by the so-called Shanghai Special Municipality Commercial Movement Committee, convening a meeting at the New World National Products Commercial Center, and listing our associations in the notice. Upon investigation, our associations have already issued a joint declaration yesterday regarding the coercion of the Shanghai Municipal Chamber of Commerce by the crowd the day before yesterday, expressing opposition to violent seizure and supporting the Shanghai Municipal Chamber of Commerce, and the newspapers have published it clearly. How could there be a fact of being listed in an illegal meeting again? It is obviously someone who has been falsely listed. Our associations cannot recognize it and hereby make a solemn statement.

▲ Telegram from the Fourth Central Committee The Municipal Chamber of Commerce sent a telegram to the First Executive Committee of the Fourth Central Committee in Nanjing yesterday, stating that the Fourth Central Committee, First Executive Committee, Nanjing, is respectfully informed that peace has been achieved, the party and the country are shining again, gathering the talents of the country to seek great plans for national salvation, pacifying the interior and resisting foreign aggression, holding the country in danger, laying the foundation for democratic politics, and bringing the people of the country into the right path. Respectfully, the Shanghai Municipal Chamber of Commerce, Hao,

▲ Telegram to the Three Commissioners The chamber, with the Central Party Headquarters, resolved to send Commissioners Chen Mingshu, Shao Lizi, and Wu Tiecheng to guide the party affairs of this city. ▲ Attending Groups and Representatives There were Zhang Yinglong of Chinese and Western Woodware, Zheng Ruohai of Department Stores, Ye Hanjun of Transportation, Qiao Tianlin of Antiques, Zhou Fumin of Fishing Boats, Zhang Zonghe of Book Covers, Fang Liao of Noodle Restaurants, Lu Peizhi of Ironware, Jin Chusong of Civilian Ships, Wang Keming of Auctions, Fei Min of Knitting, Xia Yaoxi, Yang Yuanrun of, Ye Xiaoshan of Cotton Cloth, Liu Pingsun of Cotton, Wang Fenghui of Spring Chairs, Liu Musu of Towels, Liu Guoqing of Salted Fish, Ren Yinchang of Transportation Customs Declaration, Zhu Jingzhai of Ginseng Bird's Nest, Yao Fenglin of Southern Goods, Zheng Kangnian of Flour, and the Refining Industry Sauce Industry

▲ Chairman's Report Zhang Zilian was elected chairman, and Peng Xuehai recorded the minutes. After the formalities, the chairman first reported on the purpose of the meeting and the process of the Commercial Movement Committee being organized by order. His speech stated, "Today, we are convening representatives from various industries and members of the business community to attend this meeting. The purpose is to voluntarily rise up, remove all shackles, and obtain the freedom that we deserve. Since the General Chamber of Commerce was forcibly occupied, three years have passed. We have suffered pain and oppression without being able to complain. This time, the political situation has been reorganized, and after contacting the authorities, this Commercial Movement Association, which truly represents businessmen, has been produced, with the 'power' to deal with everything. However, the purpose of convening this meeting is to develop the true meaning of all Shanghai businessmen and to discuss and resolve future directions in order to obtain its 'ability.' Therefore, this time the takeover of the Municipal Chamber of Commerce was also upright and aboveboard. Although it was not successful, it was entirely due to the shameless occupation of those people. All of us businessmen should still seek unity and deal with it together in order to achieve our goals."

▲ Key Matters Resolved (1) Restore the Shanghai Special Municipality General Chamber of Commerce, the Business Community Federations of various roads, the Nanshi Chamber of Commerce, the Zhabei Chamber of Commerce, and the Wusong Chamber of Commerce, to promote commercial movement. (2) Report Wang Yansong for abusing his party position for personal gain, oppressing the people, and destroying people's movement. It was resolved to report to the civil court and combine the cases. (4) Oppose the Shanghai Municipal Party Department and the Municipal Chamber of Commerce for violating the will of the people, restore the commercial movement, alleviate the suffering of businessmen, and promote the freedom of businessmen's will. It was resolved that the associations whose names were falsely listed should publish in the newspaper to deny all actions of the Municipal Chamber of Commerce.

▲ Temporary Motions (1) More than ten groups, including the Eyeglass Frame Industry, Department Store Industry, Knitting Industry, and Refining Industry, proposed to deny the declaration of 160 industry associations published in today's newspapers, stating that they had never agreed to it and had not stamped it. It was resolved to pass it, and the representatives who attended the meeting signed it and published it in the newspaper to deny it. (2) The Knitting, Department Store, Auction Industries, etc., proposed to initiate a "Preparatory Committee for the Restoration of the Shanghai General Chamber of Commerce" to actively work on it. It was resolved that the representatives of the various groups attending the meeting would be responsible for the preparations, and the second meeting would be convened by the Commercial Movement Committee. (3) The Ironware and Knitting Industries proposed that the representatives attending today's meeting would jointly convene all industry associations in the city to discuss reorganizing the Municipal Chamber of Commerce to express public opinion. It was resolved to pass it, and it was decided to hold the meeting at the New World at 3:00 PM on Tuesday. The meeting adjourned.

The Ten-Person Anti-Japanese Group Holds a Memorial for the Third Month of National Crisis

▲ Issued a Declaration on the National Crisis

The Ten-Person Anti-Japanese National Salvation Group held a memorial meeting for the third month of the national crisis at the YMCA auditorium at 8:00 PM the night before last. Despite the rain, there were more than 200 representatives and members who attended the meeting. Zhu Maocheng and others were elected as the presidium to open the meeting. Chen Liting delivered a speech, and then the declaration and representative meeting rules were passed, and a military research class was organized and established. At 10:00 PM, the entire group stood up, raised their hands, and read the creed: (1) Do not buy Japanese goods; (2) Do not work for the Japanese; (3) Prepare for war against Japan; (4) Promote the organization of the Ten-Person Group. The meeting adjourned in a tragic and solemn voice.
